# Welcome | Character Animation System Docs

**CAS** is a scalable, intuitive system for animating characters in Unity.

[![Logo](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Funity-assetstorev2-prd.storage.googleapis.com%2Fcdn-origin%2Fimages%2Ffavicons%2Fapple-touch-icon.png%3Fv%3D1&width=20&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=840b9b13&sv=2)Character Animation SystemUnityAssetStorechevron-right](https://assetstore.unity.com/packages/tools/animation/character-animation-system-320309)

[NextIntroduction to CASchevron-right](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/quickstart/introduction-to-cas)

Last updated 2 months ago

# Install Demo Content | Character Animation System Docs

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/quickstart/introduction-to-cas/install-demo-content#content)

Content


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To import the demo content, open **Tools/KINEMATION**, then select **CAS Demo**.

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FgexIMAfp25FxF0KaltYu%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D24f7d943-b632-4f27-8144-27501848b434&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=504ca1f7&sv=2)

Click **Download and Import**.

After download, Unity shows the import menu. Click **Import All**, or pick specific items if you prefer.

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/quickstart/introduction-to-cas/install-demo-content#scene)

Scene


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To install a demo scene, choose **Demo Scene**, select the render pipeline, and click **Download**.

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FKrFoqvBCgiCGaHHoBL4q%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3385825a-753a-4856-9ac9-6565f970d75e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3486ac83&sv=2)

Installing a demo scene.

circle-info

**Note:** Demo scenes are available for URP and HDRP only.

[NextEasy Character Setupchevron-right](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/quickstart/introduction-to-cas/easy-character-setup)

# Introduction to CAS | Character Animation System Docs

**Character Animation System** is a powerful solution that handles natural blending and procedural animation, while working alongside with Mecanim Animator.

This guide walks you through the CAS workflow using the demo content.

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/quickstart/introduction-to-cas#installing-cas)

Installing CAS


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-exclamation

**Note**: If you use other KINEMATION assets, make sure to remove:

*   KAnimationCore
    
*   ScriptableWidget
    
*   MotionWarping
    

folders before importing CAS!

**Character Animation System** is available on the Unity Asset Store. Follow these steps to import the asset to your project:

1

### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/quickstart/introduction-to-cas#open-window-package-manager)

Open Window/Package Manager

Find "My Assets" and type in "Character Animation System".

2

### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/quickstart/introduction-to-cas#import-the-asset)

Import the asset

Select the asset, download and import it to the project.

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/quickstart/introduction-to-cas#content)

Content


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Once the package is imported, you will see a "KINEMATION" folder:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FvoOC46g0hmPyvjaMjCqL%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2ffb95d6-bbad-421d-bc99-de22d7ac6179&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=be91f6ed&sv=2)

KINEMATION folder.

_Shared_ contains common modules CAS relies on, such as:

*   **KAnimationCore**: A library that provides a foundation for all animation logic.
    
*   **PropertyBindings**: A system that binds properties in the editor without any code.
    
*   **ScriptableWidget**: An editor widget used to display procedural animation modifiers.
    
*   **Character**: Kinemation Mannequin model.
    

_MotionWarping_ handles the climbing. You can learn more about it [herearrow-up-right](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/motion-warping-for-unity/)
.

CharacterAnimationSystem contains scripts and example content:

*   **Examples**: Includes Animator Controller template and example scripts (e.g., character controller).
    
*   **Scripts**: Includes all CAS main animation logic — from layered blending to procedural modifiers.
    

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/quickstart/introduction-to-cas#getting-started)

Getting Started


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This section will demonstrate how to work with **CAS** using free demo content as an example. You will learn:

*   How to install demo content.
    
*   How to set up a character.
    
*   What components CAS relies on.
    
*   How to add and control animations.
    
*   How to work with procedural animation.
    
*   How to add climbing.
    
*   What to do if something doesn't work.
    

Follow the pages below step-by-step:

[⤵️Install Demo Contentchevron-right](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/quickstart/introduction-to-cas/install-demo-content)
[🗒️Easy Character Setupchevron-right](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/quickstart/introduction-to-cas/easy-character-setup)
[⏭️After Setupchevron-right](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/quickstart/introduction-to-cas/after-setup)
[🏃‍♂️Blending and Animationschevron-right](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/quickstart/introduction-to-cas/blending-and-animations)
[🦾Proceduralchevron-right](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/quickstart/introduction-to-cas/procedural)
[⛰️Parkour and Interactionschevron-right](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/quickstart/introduction-to-cas/parkour-and-interactions)
[🛠️Troubleshootingchevron-right](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/quickstart/troubleshooting)

[PreviousWelcomechevron-left](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs)
[NextInstall Demo Contentchevron-right](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/quickstart/introduction-to-cas/install-demo-content)

# Easy Character Setup | Character Animation System Docs

circle-exclamation

**Tip:** If you’re new to CAS, use the **KINEMATION/Shared/Character** humanoid model.

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/quickstart/introduction-to-cas/easy-character-setup#basic-setup)

Basic Setup


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-info

Note: This tutorial relies on example content, so make sure to download the demo files first [Install Demo Content](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/quickstart/introduction-to-cas/install-demo-content)
.

**CAS** provides a preset-based character setup. First, add your character to the scene, right-click on it, and select "**KINEMATION/Setup CAS**":

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252F62y6qBtnCu56PQIxgEAc%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De90b0a12-2ce2-4edc-aeb4-80e5120f4db9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f6f5a1f2&sv=2)

This will open a Character Animation Setup window with preset options:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FKkKBSyvKzZBJuxkWoeP0%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7f323a2e-f48f-4dcd-bb42-9b97beceed29&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f7538574&sv=2)

Select **Basic**. More options appear if additional content is installed.

circle-check

**Tip:** Use **Manual** only if you’re experienced. It’s covered later.

Next, follow the setup steps and assign properties:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FOx3q6VFEOF2QuQuTcPMx%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3b657f14-d677-4447-8033-1ef7648df7a1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ad36a205&sv=2)

Setup window.

#### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/quickstart/introduction-to-cas/easy-character-setup#id-1.-skeleton-type)

1\. Skeleton Type

Select the type of your character model skeleton:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FqWLlU15CHhEFDU1b0Vs3%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8b79b3d4-f1e7-4f84-bd05-1b690bad557b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=706de443&sv=2)

Select your skeleton type.

CAS supports the most common model types:

*   Unreal Mannequin (UE4&UE5).
    
*   Mixamo
    
*   Character Creator (CC4, CC5)
    
*   Synty
    

For other models, choose **Default —** CAS will search bones recursively..

#### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/quickstart/introduction-to-cas/easy-character-setup#id-2.-animations)

2\. Animations

Next, we need to pick Animation Clips for our character:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FsXE2jrxIW5tGtMQ6XpKA%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D04d3fbcc-40b2-4dd5-ba98-25c017c5076b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2cb28392&sv=2)

Assign Animation Clips.

**Base Pose** is the standing idle animation. CAS uses it to compute additive motion at runtime.

**Overlay Pose** represents the current state — an item/weapon pose (e.g., torch) or a gameplay pose (e.g., injured, unarmed).

At runtime, CAS animates Overlays dynamically, turning poses into animations with natural blending.

An **Overlay Controller** serves the same role as an Overlay Pose, but adds states, transitions, and blend trees.

circle-check

**Tip:** Use Overlay Controllers for complex logic (e.g., draw/holster/attack/block as states).

circle-info

**Tip:** If both are assigned, CAS prioritizes the **Overlay Controller**.

#### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/quickstart/introduction-to-cas/easy-character-setup#id-3.-bones)

3\. Bones

Finally, assign bone references so CAS can create Procedural Animation modifiers:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252Ffo4TDAgFfXEGNDwVrr12%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd12a3c73-0664-49f3-bcb9-9eb8366e06da&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=959419ed&sv=2)

Bones.

If all bones are found, CAS shows **Good to go!**

If something’s missing, CAS warns which bones to assign manually:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FE3fEKdzK1KvqpKfLoIJu%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D25fd813a-8147-4bed-ba59-7d4a3d81a9f4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f63dee37&sv=2)

Warning example.

#### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/quickstart/introduction-to-cas/easy-character-setup#id-4.-apply-preset)

4\. Apply Preset

This adds components, ScriptableObjects, and prefabs.

circle-info

**Note**: The next page explains how these assets and prefabs are used in the system.

#### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/quickstart/introduction-to-cas/easy-character-setup#id-5.-assign-animator)

5\. Assign Animator

For **Generic** rigs, assign an **Animator Controller**:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FYtdrwEvqhem6pbSZnVTm%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D17532175-6126-4a0d-b8e7-c84a940a77af&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b3f778ef&sv=2)

Assign an Animator Controller.

[PreviousInstall Demo Contentchevron-left](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/quickstart/introduction-to-cas/install-demo-content)
[NextAfter Setupchevron-right](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/quickstart/introduction-to-cas/after-setup)

Last updated 3 months ago

# After Setup | Character Animation System Docs

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/quickstart/introduction-to-cas/after-setup#overview)

Overview


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

After applying the preset, you’ll see these ScriptableObjects and prefabs created in the current folder:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252F1UtlDU5SozMrKBjpJCMm%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D82c2f6d0-a352-4741-9124-653ed7921497&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=17f22432&sv=2)

Assets after the setup.

### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/quickstart/introduction-to-cas/after-setup#character-animation-settings)

Character Animation Settings

> CAS\_SK\_Kinemation\_Mannequin\_Humanoid

This is the main CAS data asset. It defines which Overlay and Procedural Animation settings to use:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FsCWhIEXpzC0DDjtPqPbg%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0400a8aa-1749-4f89-b727-ee6cb4282848&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d4dd1c11&sv=2)

Character Animation Settings.

**Blend Time** configures how blending should work, including blend in/out time in seconds and easing type.

**Base Pose** is the character's standing idle animation.

**Overlay Pose** is a character pose that represents the current gameplay state. It can be a weapon, item or a character's state (e.g., injured or unarmed).

The Overlay Animator serves the same role as an Overlay Pose. The only difference is that it is a separate Animator Controller with state machines and blend trees.

circle-info

**Tip**: Keep the character model separate from the main prefab. For example, a pistol overlay can consist of these states:

*   Idle Aim
    
*   Idle Rest
    
*   Tactical sprint (holding it with the right hand).
    

All these states have different blending curve values, so we can put them into a separate Overlay Controller, and CAS will handle the rest.

### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/quickstart/introduction-to-cas/after-setup#procedural-settings)

Procedural Settings

This data asset contains procedural animation modifiers that will be enabled for this character:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FmrZBd3pmFny5RScfXq1Z%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D21d41fd2-dc6c-4764-a282-c45afbc4ca6f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=38c12044&sv=2)

Procedural Animation Settings example.

**Character Prefab** is a reference to the main player prefab. It is used by animation modifiers to link your gameplay logic with the animation system.

Animation Modifiers are displayed as items in a single list. The order is important, as it defines the way modifiers will be applied at runtime. To learn more about modifiers and their use-cases, check out this page:

[🔸Animation Modifierschevron-right](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers)

### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/quickstart/introduction-to-cas/after-setup#character-skeleton-prefab)

Character Skeleton Prefab

This prefab works as a variant of your character model. It is recommended to keep character model separated from the main prefab to ensure the skeleton data is always up-to-date.

circle-check

**Tip**: If you need to modify character's hierarchy (e.g., add a camera socket Game Object), make sure to do it in the Skeleton prefab.

**CAS** relies on Character Skeleton component to get the information about character bones. It’s added to the top bone in the hierarchy (root, armature, skeleton):

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252Fo1q8nTdi4mnbeO0iiG2r%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df5d8443c-a65a-43a1-916d-c625504a5922&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8345c990&sv=2)

Skeleton component.

circle-exclamation

**Note**: Whenever a hierarchy is modified (e.g., a bone is added or removed), make sure to always update skeleton!

All main CAS components are attached to it:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FnnjMgwn6Kc7ndZlzZS0t%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D55df4f21-a9ec-40f4-88d9-967c23a042e0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9fdc4ed8&sv=2)

CAS components.

#### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/quickstart/introduction-to-cas/after-setup#character-animation-component)

Character Animation Component

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FQT0FxPa8e40DLgBD4ZRd%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df1b39a03-a320-4415-9b88-6db2391aa628&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a91c00fe&sv=2)

CAS component.

This is a central component in CAS, which is responsible for:

*   Updating current Character Animation Settings.
    
*   Controlling Layered Blending and Procedural Animation components.
    
*   Playing animations from code.
    
*   Full-body pose blending.
    

To find out more, please visit:

[🔸Character Animation Componentchevron-right](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/character-animation-component)

#### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/quickstart/introduction-to-cas/after-setup#procedural-animation-component)

Procedural Animation Component

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252F9ukMKvcFJLsM0ZfJTO5s%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D80864106-a024-4bb8-9889-30dbab56a9fc&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7edc2af6&sv=2)

Procedural Animation component.

It's responsible for creating, managing and disposing animation modifiers at runtime. To learn how to work with procedural animation, see:

[🔸Procedural Animationchevron-right](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/procedural-animation)

#### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/quickstart/introduction-to-cas/after-setup#layered-blending)

Layered Blending

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FYrpjsspGVQOQK5oOtQMn%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De10b7b26-9b2f-48cb-aa1b-90c8bd2d40dc&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e1ae4f4f&sv=2)

Layered Blending component.

This component generates animation pose at runtime, by blending Overlays (character poses, like holding a torch) with the Animator output (main Animator Controller).

**Layered Blends** define what parts of the body will be blended, and what parameters will drive that blending:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252Fx2yVhKAWzVXtocPInGp2%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D872e93e3-457f-4772-9b29-307f5824a9b7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f18850f5&sv=2)

Layered Blend and curve properties

These parameters are public float values animated by clips at runtime. Here's how it works:

*   In the editor: Properties are added to the Animation Clip using Curve Property Editor.
    
*   At runtime:
    
    *   Animation Clips update their curve values.
        
    *   Layered Blending Component uses those values for blending.
        
    

circle-check

**Tip**: Each Animation Clip tells the system how to blend it with the Animator output

To learn more about this system, check out this page:

[🔸Layered Blendingchevron-right](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/layered-blending)

### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/quickstart/introduction-to-cas/after-setup#player-controller-prefab)

Player Controller Prefab

This prefab includes the Skeleton prefab, and the Character Example Controller:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FoPbamWnGqpf6FZepRQkN%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db2af4e0e-d0e4-45df-9a26-a24d1362f0bc&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fcd61773&sv=2)

Character prefab.

This component is an example controller script, which handles:

*   Movement.
    
*   Actions and inputs.
    
*   Props (items like torch, axe, barrel and gun).
    

To find our more about example scripts, check out this page:

[🔹Example Contentchevron-right](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/example-content)

# Blending and Animations | Character Animation System Docs

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/quickstart/introduction-to-cas/blending-and-animations#overview)

Overview


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

After setup, the Overlay pose isn’t active in-game yet:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FohIEBhV2DOy7JbOVOSwG%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8f89ef91-c7bc-4e22-9080-a49886701a2f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b3df173a&sv=2)

Character standing.

The character should hold a torch, but until curve blending is set up, the Overlay isn’t visible.

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/quickstart/introduction-to-cas/blending-and-animations#adding-curves)

Adding Curves


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Right-click the Animation Clip and choose **Edit Curve Properties**:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252F42rX4EHABu8KM0J26k9d%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df52944ef-67eb-4617-816e-10459ee8f4ac&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c34a28ba&sv=2)

Curve property editor.

The Curve Property Editor adds custom float properties to a clip. Enter Play Mode and adjust the blending sliders.

To learn more about curve blending, see:

[🔸Layered Blendingchevron-right](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/layered-blending)

After you adjust the curves, the Overlay blends naturally with the Animator output:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FhPK9915lqlInpSVXu1bL%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dec2c2082-7a4f-4948-b288-ec0d2172a4c7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=47d8d060&sv=2)

Torch overlay.

* * *

The next page will focus on procedural animation workflow.

[NextProceduralchevron-right](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/quickstart/introduction-to-cas/procedural)

# Parkour and Interactions | Character Animation System Docs

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/quickstart/introduction-to-cas/parkour-and-interactions#motion-warping)

Motion Warping


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**CAS** uses Motion Warping for climbing and interactions. Motion Warping modifies root motion to match character transform with target in the game world.

This system has a separate documentation page:

[![Logo](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fkinemation.gitbook.io%2Fmotion-warping-for-unity%2F%7Egitbook%2Ficon%3Fsize%3Dsmall%26theme%3Dlight&width=20&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a09a1b42&sv=2)Welcome! | Motion Warping for Unitykinemation.gitbook.iochevron-right](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/motion-warping-for-unity/)

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/quickstart/introduction-to-cas/parkour-and-interactions#climbing-and-vaulting)

Climbing and Vaulting


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To add climbing and vaulting features, add these components to the player prefab:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FtA3KLDxEmchsUwXjAbgB%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D373454d5-df30-49d1-a46e-0c6fad03556d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c7491c0d&sv=2)

Climbing components.

[PreviousProceduralchevron-left](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/quickstart/introduction-to-cas/procedural)

# Procedural | Character Animation System Docs

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/quickstart/introduction-to-cas/procedural#overview)

Overview


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

For details, see the dedicated **Procedural Animation** page:

[🔸Procedural Animationchevron-right](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/procedural-animation)

The setup generates Procedural Animation settings that include these modifiers:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FmrZBd3pmFny5RScfXq1Z%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D21d41fd2-dc6c-4764-a282-c45afbc4ca6f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=38c12044&sv=2)

Animation Modifiers.

To learn more about each modifier, see:

[🔸Animation Modifierschevron-right](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers)

Modifier order matters — especially for IK features such as Foot IK and Step Modifier.

### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/quickstart/introduction-to-cas/procedural#ik-structure)

IK Structure

After applying the setup, these IK GameObjects are added at the character root:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FP8QJa0nFZiZg4WRknMBA%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df98c6b6f-515a-4fa3-ab44-1cbee0376b9e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=14fd1fca&sv=2)

IK Bones.

These empty GameObjects support this workflow:

1.  Copy position and rotation from real bones to the IK GameObjects (using Copy Bone modifiers).
    
2.  Apply Procedural Animation (e.g., Foot IK, Step Modifier).
    
3.  Apply IK to animate legs and arms.
    

This setup is efficient: you avoid running an expensive IK algorithm for every procedural feature.

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/quickstart/introduction-to-cas/procedural#binding-properties)

Binding Properties


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

CAS links gameplay values from your components to the animation system via [**Property Bindings**](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/property-bindings)
.

# Animation Not Playing | Character Animation System Docs

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/quickstart/troubleshooting/animation-not-playing#problem)

Problem


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When starting the game, character is not animated.

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/quickstart/troubleshooting/animation-not-playing#solution)

Solution


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Check if the Animator Controller is assigned and compatible with your character:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FYtdrwEvqhem6pbSZnVTm%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D17532175-6126-4a0d-b8e7-c84a940a77af&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b3f778ef&sv=2)

Assign Animator Controller here.

circle-info

**Note**: **Generic** animations will only work with a specific **Generic** character.

[PreviousTroubleshootingchevron-left](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/quickstart/troubleshooting)
[NextFirst-Person Camerachevron-right](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/quickstart/troubleshooting/first-person-camera)

Last updated 2 months ago

*   [Problem](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/quickstart/troubleshooting/animation-not-playing#problem)
    
*   [Solution](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/quickstart/troubleshooting/animation-not-playing#solution)

# Manual Setup | Character Animation System Docs

Add your character to the scene, right-click it, and select **KINEMATION ▸ Setup CAS**. Then choose **Manual**.

Follow these steps to configure your character for CAS:

# First-Person Camera | Character Animation System Docs

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/quickstart/troubleshooting/first-person-camera#problem)

Problem


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The camera is placed at the character's feet when in first-person view:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FX5SZVuOm2a6Akwyrjup2%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D32003734-4802-4778-8219-2836e02cb754&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7de2a445&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/quickstart/troubleshooting/first-person-camera#solution)

Solution


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Assign the **First Person Socket** in the **Character Camera** component:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FVWx6eQtguIOQbodo058l%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd76cf211-4d26-40bb-8d48-d7fd2f9b9ede&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8bd4bf4f&sv=2)

# 1.4.0 Update | Character Animation System Docs

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/quickstart/changelog/1.4.0-update#aim-at)

Aim At


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Now NPCs can look and aim at targets in your game worlds: [Aim At](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/aim-at)
.

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/quickstart/changelog/1.4.0-update#step-modifier)

Step Modifier


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step IK now correctly positions feet on the ground. To enable the new feature, just assign the right and left foot references: [Step Modifier](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/step-modifier)
.

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/quickstart/changelog/1.4.0-update#optimization)

Optimization


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Bindable Properties** now have a faster initialization thanks to the new pooling system.

# How to set up a character | Character Animation System Docs

circle-check

**Note**: Make sure the **Character Animation System** package is imported into your project!

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/tutorials/manual-setup/how-to-set-up-a-character#apply-setup)

Apply Setup


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Add your character to the scene, right-click it, and select **KINEMATION ▸ Setup CAS**:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252F62y6qBtnCu56PQIxgEAc%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De90b0a12-2ce2-4edc-aeb4-80e5120f4db9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f6f5a1f2&sv=2)

Next, select the **Manual** preset and apply it:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FT2MwO8X0x0v9zt3RUOmI%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfcb95115-9c1f-4924-9e4a-daf548bc09ee&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9760bac7&sv=2)

Click **Apply Preset**.

This adds three components to the character:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252F1wWsi9oq7L52dlnyVYFi%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Deefe5af0-b20c-4a2c-b182-7bf57d9de2d4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bd668204&sv=2)

These are main components used in the animation system.

circle-check

**Note:** Before continuing, assign an **Animator Controller** in the Animator.

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FYtdrwEvqhem6pbSZnVTm%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D17532175-6126-4a0d-b8e7-c84a940a77af&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b3f778ef&sv=2)

Assign Animtor Controller.

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/tutorials/manual-setup/how-to-set-up-a-character#create-cas-asset)

Create CAS Asset


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In the Character Animation Component menu (three dots), select **Create Animation Settings**:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252Fusp81EP8Lphnz1XgLNBO%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D66ec49bc-b57f-47f5-b721-a79a5a58ed0d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=424c834e&sv=2)

Select this option.

This creates a **ScriptableObject** in the current folder:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FCryxCG15XFqVqkg6dzmU%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4402bebf-688b-440e-9a0e-d38bebf171f1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b414aea4&sv=2)

Character Animation Settings.

_Character Animation Settings_ define properties for your weapon, item, or gameplay state (e.g., unarmed). Let's cover each property individually:

1.  **Blend Time**: Controls how these settings will be blended. Ease Mode specifies the interpolation function, and Blend In/Out Time is the time in seconds it takes to blend in or out.
    
2.  **Base Pose**: This is your idle standing animation.
    
3.  **Overlay Pose**: This is your weapon or item Animation Clip. Always assign a clip here, as it plays a crucial role in Layered Animation Blending.
    
4.  **Overlay Animator**: If you want your overlay to be more complex, you can create an Animator Controller and assign it here.
    
5.  **Procedural Settings**: These are Animation Modifiers, which will be used to dynamically animate bones. We will cover Procedural Animation in the next chapter!
    

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/tutorials/manual-setup/how-to-set-up-a-character#layered-animation-blending)

Layered animation blending


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Make sure to assign the _Base Pose_, _Overlay Pose_, and _Overlay Animator_ (optionally). Next, drag & drop your Animation Settings into the character prefab:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FdKVNLkZtVGLmSMtSWR2w%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D44165ae5-e975-4548-8021-613880115e34&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=513b40a4&sv=2)

Assign your settings here.

Next, let's see what's inside the **Layered Blending** component:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252Fxn3Fhmvy9bxPzyZe2nup%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D52c4fb00-3aa0-4300-8027-7ceae46bfac3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=97eb3da5&sv=2)

Layered Blending component.

Overlays are blended using layers using 3 unique blending parameters:

1.  **Base Weight**: This is a blend between Base Pose and Overlay. If set to 1, Ovelray will be applied for this layer, if 0 - Base Pose.
    
2.  **Additive Weight**: This value controls how much of an additive motion to apply. This is useful when we want to animate the Overlay dynamically.
    
3.  **Local Weight**: This value blends the Overlay in the local space (relative to the parent bone). This is mostly useful for fingers and toes, but sometimes we use it for arms too.
    

These values, however, are not taken directly from the component but from Animation Clips instead.

In CAS, each Animation Clip tells the system how to blend it with the Animator. To better demonstrate this concept, let's adjust the blending for our overlay.

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/tutorials/manual-setup/how-to-set-up-a-character#curve-based-animation-blending)

Curve-based animation blending


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Find your Overlay Animation Clip, right-click it, and select **Edit Curve Properties**:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FrOwznL653foQilyFaq2o%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3bc294d1-7291-4415-a711-fc978e8fe81b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cfbb6617&sv=2)

Select this option.

Once you select this option, a window with curve properties will be opened:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FmDxXBauHWFFbSOJZBRv6%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D72eb7bf8-e8ea-4acf-9482-cab5b947d9c4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e03365cd&sv=2)

Curve Property Editor.

The window lists all animatable parameters, and lets you add custom parameters. To add a custom parameter, select the "**Character Prefab**" and click the "**Add Custom Parameter**" button:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252F6WjyyEDYP6noiYiZGUwY%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6e4f7325-4bcf-43d8-9337-511c85215597&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7c0bec12&sv=2)

Custom parameters from an example prefab.

Press the **"+"** icon for base, additive, and local weights for these parameters:

1.  Layering\_LowerBody
    
2.  Layering\_Spine
    
3.  Lowering\_Head
    
4.  Lowering\_Arm\_R
    
5.  Lowering\_Arm\_L
    
6.  Lowering\_Fingers
    

Now, start the game and adjust the weight sliders! Here are some recommendations for different layers:

1.  **Layering\_LowerBody**: Set the "additiveWeight" to 1, and "baseWeight" to 0.4.
    
2.  **Layering\_Fingers**: Set the "localWeight" to 0; usually, we want fingers to be animated by the Overlay.
    

We will cover the **Layered Blending** system in more detail in the next chapters.

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/tutorials/manual-setup/how-to-set-up-a-character#blend-layers)

Blend layers


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

All blending layers are stored in the **Layered Blend** list (Layered Blending component). Every layer contains bones, which will be affected by the blending. To view and edit those bones, make sure to click the **"Edit"** button:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252F2ZB3DSazI48UeU2xZRI3%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc4374f53-8106-4c03-8bf3-9ba2a4c295c7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5aebe61b&sv=2)

Edit to open a bone chain selection.

* * *

At this point, our character setup is complete! In the next tutorial, we will learn how to add procedural animation.

[PreviousManual Setupchevron-left](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/tutorials/manual-setup)
[NextHow to set up procedural animationchevron-right](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/tutorials/manual-setup/how-to-set-up-procedural-animation)

# CAS with Unity 2022 | Character Animation System Docs

If you import CAS into a new Unity 2022 project, this error will occur:

Copy

    Assets\KINEMATION\CharacterAnimationSystem\Scripts\Runtime\Playables\AnimationLayeringJobs.cs(27,16): error CS0246: The type or namespace name 'NativeReference<>' could not be found (are you missing a using directive or an assembly reference?)

To fix this, make sure to update CAS to the latest version and install the **Collections** package: **Package Manager ▸ Unity Registry ▸ Collections:**

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FT4gSHnflRjAa3b23iSCC%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc6c5eedc-d2e8-49d9-996e-cc8caf0d27c4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9edde18b&sv=2)

[PreviousHow to set up procedural animationchevron-left](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/tutorials/manual-setup/how-to-set-up-procedural-animation)
[NextArchitecturechevron-right](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/architecture)

# How to set up procedural animation | Character Animation System Docs

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/tutorials/manual-setup/how-to-set-up-procedural-animation#create-procedural-animation-settings)

Create Procedural Animation Settings


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

On the character prefab, open **Procedural Animation** (three dots) and choose **Create Procedural Asset**.

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FxiXkWf9mgw8DQkoU7ZYW%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3687d118-55fc-44e1-894f-7b75a75667f7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=34e1c49d&sv=2)

Create Procedural Animation Settings.

**Procedural Animation Settings** list the Animation Modifiers applied to the skeleton at runtime:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FraqmHl19c9F1lzcoMq9Q%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dacdee0d6-d992-4528-8bf3-ece75fded86b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=29b3b28b&sv=2)

Procedural Animation Settings.

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/tutorials/manual-setup/how-to-set-up-procedural-animation#animation-modifiers)

Animation Modifiers


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Assign **Character Prefab** — the main player prefab used in-game. If you don’t have one yet, drag the scene character into the current folder to create a prefab.

circle-check

**Tip:** This prefab’s structure is used to bind gameplay data to Animation Modifiers.

After assigning the prefab, add Animation Modifiers:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FBeAv9KMUIM2Dh5J7dqZ6%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9063e288-8009-4669-82eb-9da7f038d0eb&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8edb2793&sv=2)

Modifiers.

You can add multiple modifiers of the same type (e.g., several **Modify Bone** or **Two Bone IK**). Choose any combination you need.

circle-check

**Note**: For details, see [Animation Modifiers](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers)
.

Finally, assign your **Procedural Animation Settings** in the **Character Animation Settings**:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252F1kHBY8YHlkwPDRNHymTJ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D45e1dea8-07f4-4c13-8dcf-998274d242cb&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a776a54f&sv=2)

Assign the PA here.

[PreviousHow to set up a characterchevron-left](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/tutorials/manual-setup/how-to-set-up-a-character)
[NextCAS with Unity 2022chevron-right](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/tutorials/cas-with-unity-2022)

# Architecture | Character Animation System Docs

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/architecture#overview)

Overview


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Character Animation System relies on three systems:

1.  [**Layered Blending**](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/layered-blending)
     for naturally combining animations.
    
2.  [**Procedural Animation**](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/procedural-animation)
     for dynamically modifying bones after the blending.
    
3.  [**Property Bindings**](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/property-bindings)
     for linking gameplay data with the animation system.
    

[**Character Animation Component**](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/character-animation-component)
 controls execution for:

[🔸Layered Blendingchevron-right](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/layered-blending)
[🔸Procedural Animationchevron-right](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/procedural-animation)

circle-check

**Tip**: All custom animation logic is implemented based on the [Playables APIarrow-up-right](https://docs.unity3d.com/6000.1/Documentation/Manual/Playables.html)
.

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FE1u5lzegQvHpdinZmq1z%252FUntitled%2520Diagram.drawio.svg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D83b25eb5-7840-4977-b969-a80919420eb1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f96587ed&sv=2)

Playable graph structure in CAS.

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/architecture#base-pose-and-overlays)

Base Pose and Overlays


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Base Pose** is the standing idle animation. This pose will be subtracted from the Animator output and added to the character Overlay as a dynamic additive animation.

**Overlay Pose** is a weapon, item, or action character pose. In other words, it is a pose that we want to animate dynamically at runtime.

circle-check

**Example**: A character holding a rifle can be used as an Overlay.

An **Overlay Animator Controller** serves the same role as an Overlay Pose, and adds states and transitions for blending multiple overlays.

circle-check

**Example**: To add sword draw, idle, and holster overlays, we can create a new Animator Controller that will support these states

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FuzdkUrq0RkoEeUAg5ZDy%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D424698a1-abd2-4d1c-80f2-ad0a1eb7abe1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=22e436f2&sv=2)

Overlay Animator Controller example.

To access active Overlay Animator Controller in code, use:

circle-check

**Tip**: Use this logic to update parameters in Overlay Controllers.

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/architecture#overlay-animation-slot)

Overlay Animation Slot


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This is a point in the playable graph where animations are played from code. You can learn more about slots and how to play animations from code here:

[🔸Animation Assetchevron-right](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-asset)
[🔸Character Animation Componentchevron-right](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/character-animation-component)

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/architecture#animator-output)

Animator Output


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This is the output pose from the Animator Controller. CAS doesn’t access the Animator directly — it uses the current character pose.

circle-check

**Tip**: It's possible to use **CAS** with custom Playables packages, like Animation Rigging, for example.

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/architecture#procedural-animation)

Procedural Animation


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

# Character Animation Component | Character Animation System Docs

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/character-animation-component#overview)

Overview


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Character Animation Component is the central MonoBehaviour in CAS. It handles:

1.  Applying [Layered Blending](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/layered-blending)
     and [Procedural Animation](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/procedural-animation)
    .
    
2.  Pose blending.
    
3.  Animation Slots to play clips at runtime.
    

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FJTOLQxRGTkSDTZO4sRRp%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D606f4ca5-c705-4295-b717-323b4f8477a8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6af7bb4&sv=2)

Character Animation Component.

This component uses the **Character Animation Settings** asset to update the active Overlay and Procedural Animation modifiers.

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/character-animation-component#character-animation-settings)

Character Animation Settings


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FsCWhIEXpzC0DDjtPqPbg%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0400a8aa-1749-4f89-b727-ee6cb4282848&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d4dd1c11&sv=2)

Character Animation Settings.

circle-check

**Tip:** Create a new CAS asset via **Create ▸ KINEMATION ▸ CAS ▸ CAS Settings**.

*   **Blend Time** — **Ease Mode** sets the interpolation; **Blend In/Out Time** sets the seconds to blend in/out.
    
*   **Base Pose** — the standing idle animation.
    
*   **Overlay Pose** — the weapon/item clip. Always assign this; Layered Blending depends on it.
    
*   **Overlay Animator** — assign an Animator Controller for complex overlay logic (states, transitions, blend trees).
    
*   **Procedural Settings** — Animation Modifiers that dynamically animate bones.
    

circle-info

**Tip**: This asset can serve as a profile or a preset for a weapon, item or a gameplay situation. It's recommended to create CAS assets for different scenarios and update them at runtime.

You can update **Character Animation Settings** at runtime:

Example usage:

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/character-animation-component#pose-blending)

Pose Blending


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The component supports on-demand pose blending:

When called, it caches the current pose on the animation thread, then blends from the cached to the live pose starting next frame.

A common use case is switching Animator Controllers, since Unity doesn’t natively smooth transitions between different Animators.

circle-exclamation

**Note:** `RequestPoseBlending` is called automatically when you use `UpdateAnimationSettings`.

* * *

The next page explains how to use Animation Slots and play clips from code.

[PreviousArchitecturechevron-left](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/architecture)
[NextAnimation Assetchevron-right](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-asset)

Last updated 2 months ago

*   [Overview](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/character-animation-component#overview)
    
*   [Character Animation Settings](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/character-animation-component#character-animation-settings)
    
*   [Pose Blending](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/character-animation-component#pose-blending)
    

CharacterAnimationComponent.cs

Copy

    public void UpdateAnimationSettings(CharacterAnimationSettings newSettings)

ExampleComponent.cs

Copy

    [SerializeField] private CharacterAnimationSettings torchSettings;
    
    private CharacterAnimationComponent _characterAnimation;
    
    private void Start()
    {
        _characterAnimation = GetComponent<CharacterAnimationComponent>();
    }
    
    private void OnTorchEquipped()
    {
        if (_characterAnimation != null)
        {
            _characterAnimation.UpdateAnimationSettings(torchSettings);
        }
    }
    

CharacterAnimationComponent.cs

Copy

    public void RequestPoseBlending(BlendTime blendTime)

# Animation Asset | Character Animation System Docs

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-asset#overview)

Overview


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

An Animation Asset is a **ScriptableObject** that stores an Animation Clip and the properties that define how CAS plays it:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FvcfpbBk0swZwn3CDZoPu%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da4cc314c-18cc-48bb-b357-0222674dadfa&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bfeae9bb&sv=2)

Animation Asset example.

*   **Clip** — the Animation Clip to play.
    
*   **Mask** — the bones affected by this animation.
    
*   **Ease Mode** — easing function for blend in/out.
    
*   **Blend In/Out Time** — seconds to blend in/out.
    
*   **Play Rate** — playback speed multiplier.
    
*   **Is Additive** — apply the animation additively.
    
*   **Auto Blend Out** — automatically blend out on completion.
    
*   **Slot** — where to play this animation in the layered blending.
    

circle-check

**Tip**: Create a new Animation Asset via **Create ▸ KINEMATION ▸ CAS ▸ Animation Asset.**

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-asset#animation-slots)

Animation Slots


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Animation Slots define where a clip is applied in the animation graph. By default, there are three:

*   **Default Overlay**
    
*   **Overlay**
    
*   **Full Body**
    

Each slot applies at a different stage of the graph.

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FHFJbmwjosufbQG2LwGoE%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df7538cf9-98b2-4d8f-9e67-a4b577bee7d0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7dfb5506&sv=2)

Slots.

#### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-asset#default-overlay)

Default Overlay

Use for general animations when you want to preserve **Dynamic Bones**.

circle-check

**Example:** If a Dynamic Bone positions the weapon and you want its result preserved, use **Default Overlay**.

#### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-asset#overlay)

Overlay

Applied after **Default Overlay**. Use when the animation should affect **Dynamic Bones**.

circle-check

**Example:** For a reload animation that should drive the weapon’s Dynamic Bone, use **Overlay**.

#### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-asset#full-body)

Full Body

Applied after blending; affects the whole character pose. Use for full-body animations (e.g., climbing).

#### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-asset#post-full-body)

Post Full Body

Applied after **Full Body**; plays on top of the final character pose.

circle-check

**Example:** Parkour motions, like climbing or vaulting.

Use the **Character Animation Component** to play or stop an Animation Asset:

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-asset#custom-events)

Custom Events


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can bind custom events to an animation asset by supplying an array of `AnimationMixerEvent` objects.

Example:

The AnimationMixerEvent struct has a very simple constructor.

The callback has the following signature.

*   `animationAsset` — The animation asset that triggers the event.
    
*   `normalizedTime` — The normalized playback time **\[0..1\]** when the event is triggered.
    

[PreviousCharacter Animation Componentchevron-left](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/character-animation-component)
[NextLayered Blendingchevron-right](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/layered-blending)

Last updated 16 days ago

*   [Overview](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-asset#overview)
    
*   [Animation Slots](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-asset#animation-slots)
    
*   [Custom Events](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-asset#custom-events)
    

CharacterAnimationComponent.cs

Copy

    public virtual bool PlayAnimation(AnimationAsset newAnimation, float startTime = 0f);
    public virtual void StopAnimation(float blendOutTime = 0f)

ExampleClassHere.cs

Copy

    [SerializeField] private AnimationAsset animationToPlay;
    private CharacterAnimationComponent _characterAnimation;
    
    private void Start()
    {
        _characterAnimation = GetComponent<CharacterAnimationComponent>();
    }
    
    // Your function that plays an animation.
    private void PlayAnimation()
    {
        _characterAnimation.PlayAnimation(animationToPlay);
    }

Copy

    private void YourCallback(AnimationAsset animationAsset, float normalizedTime)
    {
        Debug.Log($"Animation: {animation.name}, Normalized time: {time}");
    }
    
    private void YourMethodHere()
    {
        _characterAnimation.PlayAnimation(animationToPlay, 0f, new []
        {
            new AnimationMixerEvent(YourCallback, 0f),
            new AnimationMixerEvent((animationAsset, time) => 
            {
                Debug.Log($"Animation: {animation.name}, Normalized time: {time}");
            }, 0f)
        });
    }

Copy

    //Callback will be invoked at the normalizedTime.
    public AnimationMixerEvent(AnimationTimeEventDelegate callback, float normalizedTime)

Copy

    public delegate void AnimationTimeEventDelegate(AnimationAsset animationAsset, float normalizedTime)

# Procedural Animation | Character Animation System Docs

The **Procedural Animation Component** creates, updates, and disposes animation modifiers:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FP1SrhWseuMgcAqaP5JyG%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db22e0be8-4ee6-4a0c-93e1-6e1076db37f6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bfae2ab&sv=2)

Procedural logic in CAS is based on Animation Modifiers. These modular ScriptableObjects live in a **Procedural Animation Settings (PAS)** asset:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FutyRbn0EG7DKtJSlAMcF%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D849c0e80-6960-4962-8d7d-724950d6842d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3ece648&sv=2)

Modifiers.

circle-check

**Tip:** Create a PAS via **Create ▸ KINEMATION ▸ CAS ▸ Procedural Animation**.

Modifier order defines how procedural features apply to the pose.

To add a new modifier, click the **Add Animation Modifier** and navigate the categories:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252F3m7xoS8DwmDq7CDQqLBR%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd7813b3e-1441-4170-b895-de0549b96577&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=96164a67&sv=2)

Selecting a modifier.

[PreviousLayered Blendingchevron-left](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/layered-blending)
[NextAnimation Modifierschevron-right](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers)

# Modify Bone Chain | Character Animation System Docs

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/modify-bone-chain#overview)

Overview


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Modify Bone Chain** has the same function as Modify Bone, but it applies translation and rotation to a chain of bones.

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FYI2ttfxMQIknmMaJBUu2%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddaf29646-9010-4eec-9643-ee927ecf4c22&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=424cb8aa&sv=2)

Modify Bone Chain.

*   **Chain To Modify** — bones that will be affected.
    
*   **Position** — translation offset; it's possible to bind an external value here.
    
*   **Rotation** — rotation offset; it's possible to bind an external value here.
    
*   **Space** — what space the offset will be applied in.
    
*   **Mode** — whether to add or replace bone transforms.
    

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/modify-bone-chain#use-cases)

Use-cases


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This modifier is useful when there's a need to rotate multiple bones at once. For example, the FPS Add-on uses this feature to implement trigger discipline:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FKMBTlaAmeTqnj35MiLmx%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df2d87cc7-b6b9-48dc-9413-190b8b0f26e2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d025443f&sv=2)

circle-check

**Tip**: When a character is sprinting, this layer will apply 45 degree rotation around the Z axis for the right index finger bones.

[PreviousModify Bonechevron-left](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/modify-bone)
[NextLook Modifierchevron-right](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/look-modifier)

Last updated 3 months ago

*   [Overview](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/modify-bone-chain#overview)

# Simple Animation Player | Character Animation System Docs

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/simple-animation-player#overview)

Overview


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This component is used to dynamically play animations from code:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FBaE7mXgyGkhdHd0NVz0j%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6c225725-8da1-4343-bfbb-ff975219a9ca&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=707b7b2&sv=2)

*   **Use Animator** — if true, animations will be played on top of existing Animator Controller.
    
*   **Default Clip Pose** — this clip will be used as the default pose. It's only used when **Use Animator** is false.
    

Simple Animation Player is added to the same Game Object as the Animator component:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252Foh1Rp24I2z4oqi7j3c4o%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfbbd17fd-f2f6-4b48-9536-9c3d8a9d96a1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dec453c&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/simple-animation-player#use-cases)

Use-cases


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

It's primarily used for animated props like weapons. Instead of creating Animator Controllers for every item, this component lets you play animations from code:

circle-check

**Tip**: [Animation Assets](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-asset)
 are used for more granular control over the clip speed and blending settings.

Here's an example code snippet that shows how Simple Animation Player can be used to play animations for a weapon:

[PreviousDynamic Boneschevron-left](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/dynamic-bones)
[NextState Behaviourschevron-right](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/state-behaviours)

Last updated 3 months ago

*   [Overview](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/simple-animation-player#overview)
    
*   [Use-cases](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/simple-animation-player#use-cases)
    

Copy

    public bool PlayAnimation(AnimationAsset newAnimation, float startTime = 0f).

WeaponExample.cs

Copy

    [SerializedField] private AnimationClip weaponIdlePose;
    private SimpleAnimationPlayer _animationPlayer;
    
    private void Start()
    {
        // 1. Try to get the animation player.
        _animationPlayer = GetComponent<SimpleAnimationPlayer>();
        
        // 2. Play weapon base pose
        if(_animationPlayer != null) _animationPlayer.PlayBasePlayable(weaponIdlePose);
        
    }
    
    private void PlayReloadAnimation(AnimationAsset reloadAnimation)
    {
        // 3. Play custom animations on demand.
        if(_animationPlayer != null) _animationPlayer.PlayAnimation(reloadAnimation);
    }
