# State Behaviours | Character Animation System Docs

[State Behavioursarrow-up-right](https://docs.unity3d.com/6000.2/Documentation/Manual/StateMachineBehaviours.html)
 are components added to state in the animator controller.

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/state-behaviours#set-float)

Set Float


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FvY9hKUGOqK7r1gkbVeRv%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D212508be-93ac-4a56-8cc2-171bb2815a87&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b9ee38d8&sv=2)

This behaviour sets a float parameter to a user-specifed value, taking transition time into account.

circle-check

**Tip**: For example, if transition lasts for 0.25s, then it will take 0.25s to blend in new float value.

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/state-behaviours#play-step)

Play Step


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FbqeXJF5jEw8x7VGy3g7X%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2d279402-0315-44e0-9f90-47fe67828fa1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b6815605&sv=2)

This behaviour plays [procedural steps](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/step-modifier)
 when entering or leaving the state. Use it to avoid feet sliding when playing states.

[PreviousSimple Animation Playerchevron-left](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/simple-animation-player)
[NextProperty Bindingschevron-right](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/property-bindings)

Last updated 3 months ago

*   [Set Float](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/state-behaviours#set-float)
    
*   [Play Step](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/state-behaviours#play-step)

# Layered Blending | Character Animation System Docs

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/layered-blending#overview)

Overview


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/layered-blending#component)

Component

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FrOw3JSu15wbSvMEg6OuM%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7078eb9d-e508-431c-ab25-74486bd277f7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9be6f0ff&sv=2)

Layered Blending Component.

Layered Blending combines the main Animator output with the Overlay.

*   **Global Weight** — controls the overall influence of the component.
    
*   **Always Animate Poses** — evaluates Overlays every frame. Disable to process them once for better performance.
    
*   **Link Animator Parameters** — updates parameters in the current Overlay Animator Controller using values from the main Animator.
    
*   **Apply Root Motion** — toggles root motion.
    

circle-info

**Tip**: Click "Generate Layered Blends" when skeleton hierarchy is updated - it will re-create Layered Blends elements.

### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/layered-blending#layering)

Layering

Layered Blends define which body parts are affected and which float parameters drive the blending.

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252Fxn3Fhmvy9bxPzyZe2nup%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D52c4fb00-3aa0-4300-8027-7ceae46bfac3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=97eb3da5&sv=2)

Layered Blends.

**Generated bone chains (by default):**

*   Lower Body (legs and pelvis)
    
*   Spine
    
*   Head
    
*   Left Arm / Right Arm
    
*   Fingers
    

circle-check

**Tip:** You can create custom bone chains. Click "**+"** and then "**Edit"** to pick bones.

Each blending layer exposes three weights:

*   **Base Weight** — mixes Base Pose vs. Overlay on this layer
    
*   **Additive Weight** — scales additive motion on this layer
    
*   **Local Weight** — blends the Overlay in local space (useful for fingers/toes; sometimes arms)
    

All layering parameters are Animation Curves that are attached to an Overlay clip. At runtime, Animation Clips update their values, hence telling the system how to blend them with the main Animator output.

circle-check

**Tip**: This gives greater flexibility to any Animation Clip used in the Overlay, as each animation can have a unique blending with the locomotion.

#### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/layered-blending#overlay-parameters)

Overlay Parameters

You can propagate custom float parameters from the base Animator to Overlays using **Overlay Parameters**. Each overlay parameter acts as an additive offset that CAS applies on top of the base value at runtime.

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252F7UDAxwXE29wYqMqJ16Xy%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6f156a8d-68e1-422c-9ab3-8b20475ec6f7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f3260b7c&sv=2)

1.  **Add a parameter and bind a float** Add a float parameter to the **Overlay Parameters** list. At runtime, CAS will _add_ this float to the current value of the corresponding Animator parameter.
    
2.  **Example: Disabling IK while climbing** To disable hand IK when the character is climbing:
    
    *   In your climbing animation, add a float parameter named `Enable_HandL_IK`.
        
    *   Set its value to **\-1**.
        
    *   Add `Enable_HandL_IK` to the **Overlay Parameters** list in CAS.
        
    
    When the climbing overlay is active, CAS adds `-1` to the current `Enable_HandL_IK` value, effectively masking it out (disabling the IK for that hand).
    

This mechanism lets the base Animator drive the parameter while Overlays locally adjust or override it.

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/layered-blending#curve-property-editor)

Curve Property Editor


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/layered-blending#adding-curves)

Adding Curves

To add layering properties to an Animation Clip, right-click on the animation and select "**Edit Curve Properties**":

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FrOwznL653foQilyFaq2o%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3bc294d1-7291-4415-a711-fc978e8fe81b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cfbb6617&sv=2)

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252F42rX4EHABu8KM0J26k9d%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df52944ef-67eb-4617-816e-10459ee8f4ac&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c34a28ba&sv=2)

Curve Property Editor.

Use "**+**" to add, and "**\-**" to remove a property.

The toggle box is used to switch between the slider and free-range property. The latter is useful when a value has to be specifically out of \[0;1\] slider's range.

All custom float properties are added to Animation Clips as curves. It's possible to edit the curve directly, instead of using the float field or slider. Right-click on the parameter and select "Curve Mode":

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FvZKiytjOgLmBOWQczq83%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1e57d057-7289-45f7-9cf7-5a9ce8974969&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8597bfc1&sv=2)

Different editing modes.

**Curve Mode** means the property will be represented as a curve.

**Value Mode** means that the property will be a constant curve with a value assigned in the slider or float field.

### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/layered-blending#blending-parameters)

Blending Parameters

Layered Blending provides these float properties by default:

*   Layering\_LowerBody
    
*   Layering\_Spine
    
*   Layering\_Head
    
*   Layering\_Arm\_R
    
*   Layering\_Arm\_L
    
*   Layering\_Fingers
    

These additional floats are available for use with [Procedural Animation](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/procedural-animation)
 and IK:

*   Mask\_Procedural\_Animation
    
*   Weapon\_Bone\_Weight
    
*   Mask\_Look\_Rotation
    
*   Mask\_Attach\_Hand
    
*   Enable\_HandR\_IK / Enable\_HandL\_IK
    
*   Enable\_FootR\_IK / Enable\_FootL\_IK
    

Each new blending parameter is authored as a float curve in the animation clip and bound to a corresponding public `float` property. At runtime, Unity creates and resolves these bindings, allowing clips to drive our layering properties. Those values are then forwarded to the **Layered Blending** component.

Unity has an important limitation: it does **not** automatically reset curve-bound values each frame. As a result, if an animation clip sets `Enable_HandR_IK` to `1`, that value can persist even after the clip stops playing. These “stale” values may continue influencing blending and lead to incorrect results.

To prevent this, manually reset the layering curves in your main **Animator Controller**:

1.  Create a new default layer (first in the layer order).
    
2.  Drag the `Curves_Default` clip from **CAS** into that layer.
    

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252F0lGukkmUg6sORFzSK3uS%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfa82b828-fad6-4aa9-983a-6da38d1510d3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cd7d6ef3&sv=2)

Drag this clip as a default state.

circle-info

**Tip:** This ensures all blending parameters are driven back to `0` every frame, eliminating issues caused by lingering values.

### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/layered-blending#custom-properties)

Custom Properties

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252F6WjyyEDYP6noiYiZGUwY%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6e4f7325-4bcf-43d8-9337-511c85215597&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7c0bec12&sv=2)

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FpInYCoSFBkJxl5yi4p5t%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2b78074b-11b7-44c6-94e0-ff6b67d9aefc&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b1b9dcf8&sv=2)

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FhMXsqJlRXHy6JJKg8wS5%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4117658b-edf3-4fd7-84ee-deb43a534fc3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e9649900&sv=2)

# Dynamic Bones | Character Animation System Docs

**Dynamic Bone** is a bone or a Game Object that allows animating bones in a different space. To make a Dynamic Bone, add the Dynamic Bone component:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FFKikRKJKQYZUN5Ca1czb%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D65d2bf76-e9af-4899-8793-4d4e2995a2c1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cbca0e69&sv=2)

Dynamic Bone component.

*   **Target**: This bone will be the animation source.
    
*   **Update Mode**: Whether to affect this bone by animations.
    
*   **Apply Blending**: Whether to include this bone in blending.
    

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/dynamic-bones#how-to-use-it)

How to use it


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Dynamic Bones are quite useful when we want to take one bone's animated transform and move it to a different space.

For example, let's say we have a weapon bone, which is not parented to the right hand. To fix this, we can create a Dynamic Bone that will be parented to the right hand, targeting the gun bone:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FIyDkXA2VD1dwH7UzHU90%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7a154b30-4fc8-44ef-923e-d5889e07e426&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9d48de9e&sv=2)

Dynamic Bone example.

This Dynamic Bone will be animated just as ik\_hand\_gun, but as if it were parented to the right hand. As a result, our weapon will be positioned correctly at all times.

Another example is left-hand IK. Instead of using a transform to attach the left hand, we can create a Dynamic Bone and parent it to the right hand:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FxuvpCrVsvvSXf5NXcJ39%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8184312b-43f1-40a8-8ddb-696a4b4db6be&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bd30eea2&sv=2)

Left hand example.

This will make the Dynamic Bone take the left-hand transform, but still be parented to the right hand, just as if it were attached to it!

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/dynamic-bones#how-update-modes-work)

How update modes work


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This property defines when the Dynamic Bone will be updated:

*   **Default**: after the "Overlay Animation Slot" in the [Playable Graph](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/architecture)
    .
    
*   **Preserve Overlay**: after the "Overlay Pose" and before the "Overlay Animation Slot".
    

In most cases, the update mode should be set to "Default", unless there is a need always to keep the original pose.

[PreviousAim Atchevron-left](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/aim-at)
[NextSimple Animation Playerchevron-right](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/simple-animation-player)

Last updated 7 months ago

*   [How to use it](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/dynamic-bones#how-to-use-it)
    
*   [How update modes work](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/dynamic-bones#how-update-modes-work)

# Character Skeleton | Character Animation System Docs

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/character-skeleton#component)

Component


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Character Skeleton** is used to store bone hierarchy and get bone references at runtime:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252F1byeL3QiQ88n1HzxPngt%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D73e87b5b-5691-46ec-9c88-807bdd6c496b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4d2457d5&sv=2)

Character Skeleton component.

*   **Skeleton** is a list of all bone transforms.
    
*   **Skeleton Bone Chains** lists auto-generated bone chains for different parts of the body.
    

circle-check

**Tip**: To update the hierarchy, click the "Update Skeleton" button and apply changes to the prefab.

This component is added to the root bone (e.g., root, armature, skeleton, etc.)m and it's used by Animation Modifiers and Layered Blending to select bones in the editor.

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/character-skeleton#irigprovider)

IRigProvider


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This simple interface plays a crucial role in editor bone selection:

**KRigElement** is a struct that has 2 fields:

*   name (string).
    
*   index (int).
    
*   depth (int).
    

It implements a custom drawer that tries to get a Rig Provider from the parent. For example, Procedural Animation Settings asset has a reference to the Character Prefab. When a bone is picked, it will try to get the Character Skeleton component and return the array of rig elements.

### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/character-skeleton#api-reference)

API Reference

chevron-rightProperties[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/character-skeleton#properties)

chevron-rightMethods[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/character-skeleton#methods)

[PreviousProperty Bindingschevron-left](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/property-bindings)
[NextExample Contentchevron-right](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/example-content)

Last updated 4 months ago

*   [Component](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/character-skeleton#component)
    
*   [IRigProvider](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/character-skeleton#irigprovider)
    
*   [API Reference](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/character-skeleton#api-reference)
    

Copy

    public interface IRigProvider
    {
        public KRigElement[] GetHierarchy();
    }

Copy

    // Returns a list of all bones in the hierarchy.
    public List<CharacterSkeletonBone> SkeletonBones => skeleton;
    
    // Returns all bone chains in this skeleton.
    public List<KRigElementChain> ElementChains => skeletonBoneChains;

Copy

    
    // Recursively finds all child transforms of the root bone.
    public void UpdateSkeleton()
    
    // Returns all rig elements in this skeleton.
    public KRigElement[] GetRigElements()
    
    // Returns a rig element by a Transform reference.
    public KRigElement GetRigElement(Transform bone)
    
    // Returns a rig element by name.
    public KRigElement GetRigElement(string boneName)
    
    // Returns a skeleton bone by index.
    public CharacterSkeletonBone GetSkeletonBoneByIndex(int index)
    
    // Returns all boen transforms in ths skeleton.
    public Transform[] GetTransformHierarchy()
    
    // Returns a bone transform by name.
    public Transform GetBoneTransform(string boneName)
    
    // Returns a bone transform by rig element.
    // It will try to use element index first.
    public Transform GetBoneTransform(KRigElement element)
    
    // Cached all bone transforms.
    // This shouldn't be used at runtime.
    public void CacheSkeletonPose()
    
    // Applies bone transform cache.
    // This shouldn't be used at runtime.
    public void RestoreCachedSkeletonPose()

# Animation Modifiers | Character Animation System Docs

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers#overview)

Overview


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

An **Animation Modifier** defines procedural animation settings and logic. Modifiers reside in the [Procedural Animation Settingsarrow-up-right](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/procedural-animation)
 and are placed in a list. You can add multiple modifiers of the same type to the settings:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FzqF5ZZNcQmt181GmjR3Y%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daebadbe6-ad2a-4dcd-b73c-2f8b22e68580&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dbe41f94&sv=2)

Animation Modifiers.

Each modifier has a Gizmo-toggle button—use it to enable or disable the UI. This is useful for making adjustments and debugging.

circle-check

**Tip**: Modifiers are applied at runtime in the same order as their position in the list.

All modifiers consist of 2 parts:

1.  **Settings**: a ScriptableObject that contains data (e.g., bone references).
    
2.  **Animation Job**: a runtime-only struct that executes the logic (e.g., applies inverse kinematics).
    

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FTdrfAyjpgpLvwQsquGRU%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D51f9e946-6b50-4cec-ac64-d560a1925b99&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f163dfef&sv=2)

IK modifiers example.

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers#weight-overrides)

Weight Overrides


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This feature provides more granular control over how modifiers are applied at runtime, using custom float properties:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FlkRbjc4yE9yGqX0n5FnI%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D88d04d1e-9ee0-4d0c-998e-f6d2e908498e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=38268128&sv=2)

Weight Override.

*   **Weight** — a float property to control the influence of this modifier.
    
*   **Is Mask** — if enabled, the final value is computed as `1f - Weight`.
    
*   **In Range Min** and **Max** — used to remap the Weight value. For example, if the Weight value is in a range other than \[0, 1\], specify the min and max values of the Weight range.
    

circle-check

**Tip**: You can add multiple overrides to the same modifier. In this case, their outputs are multiplied. If one of the overrides is zero, the final value is zero.

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers#animation-modifier-settings)

Animation Modifier Settings


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**AnimationModifierSettings** is a base class for all modifier settings in the system:

chevron-rightInheritance and Interfaces[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers#inheritance-and-interfaces)

*   **IRigProvider**: This interface is used to provide a skeleton hierarchy for editor widgets (e.g., bone or bone chain selection).
    
*   **IBindableContext**: This interface provides a GameObject context for [https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/property-bindings](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/property-bindings)
    .
    

chevron-rightFields[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers#fields)

*   **characterPrefab**: A reference to the player prefab.
    
*   **alpha**: A value that controls the influence of this modifier.
    
*   **weightOverrides**: Additional float parameters to adjust alpha at runtime. This section is useful when multiple values should affect the influence of a modifier (e.g., blending it out when playing a specific animation).
    

chevron-rightMethods[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers#methods)

*   **InitializeOnLoad()**: Called when the game starts. This callback is used to build **Property Bindings**.
    
*   **CreateAnimationJob()**: Called when _Procedural Animation Settings_ are initialized and returns an instance of an Animation Job that executes the logic.
    
*   **GetContext()**: Returns a context GameObject for **Property Bindings**.
    
*   **GetHierarchy()**: Returns an array of all bones in the skeleton.
    

Although the Modifier Settings class is derived from a ScriptableObject, it is not typically instantiated as an asset in the project.

**By default**, all modifiers exist only in the Procedural Animation Settings and shouldn't be accessed from the outside.

circle-info

**Note**: Animation Jobs run their logic on the animation thread, so modifying their data at runtime may result in unexpected behaviors.

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers#animation-modifier-job)

Animation Modifier Job


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

An **Animation Modifier Job** is a struct that executes animation logic. All jobs in the Character Animation System implement 2 interfaces:

1.  **IAnimationJob**: an interface provided by Unity's Playables API.
    
2.  **IAnimationModifierJob**: an interface provided by the Character Animation System.
    

chevron-rightIAnimationModifierJob[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers#ianimationmodifierjob)

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers#animation-modifier-pooling)

Animation Modifier Pooling


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**CAS** reuses already allocated modifiers when updating animation settings. When this occurs, the system calls **Initialize()** and recreates the **AnimationScriptPlayable** linked to this **Animation Modifier**.

[PreviousProcedural Animationchevron-left](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/procedural-animation)
[NextCopy Bonechevron-right](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/copy-bone)

Last updated 3 months ago

*   [Overview](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers#overview)
    
*   [Weight Overrides](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers#weight-overrides)
    
*   [Animation Modifier Settings](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers#animation-modifier-settings)
    
*   [Animation Modifier Job](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers#animation-modifier-job)
    
*   [Animation Modifier Pooling](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers#animation-modifier-pooling)
    

Copy

    public class AnimationModifierSettings : ScriptableObject, IRigProvider, IBindableContext

Copy

    [ShowStandalone] public GameObject characterPrefab;
    [Range(0f, 1f)] public float alpha = 1f;
    [Unfold] public List<WeightOverride> weightOverrides = new List<WeightOverride>();

Copy

    public virtual void InitializeOnLoad();
    public virtual IAnimationModifierJob CreateAnimationJob();
    public GameObject GetContext();
    public KRigElement[] GetHierarchy();

IAnimationModifierJob.cs

Copy

    public interface IAnimationModifierJob
    {
        /// <summary>
        /// Sets up a job. Called on the main thread when a new profile is linked.
        /// </summary>
        /// <param name="jobData">General job data.</param>
        /// <param name="settings">Procedural animation asset.</param>
        public void Initialize(ModifierJobData jobData, AnimationModifierSettings settings);
        
        /// <summary>
        /// Creates a new AnimationScriptPlayable based on the Animation Job.
        /// </summary>
        /// <param name="graph">Main Playable Graph.</param>
        /// <param name="source">Source Playable.</param>
        /// <returns></returns>
        public AnimationScriptPlayable CreatePlayable(PlayableGraph graph);
        
        /// <summary>
        /// Returns active Animator Layer Settings.
        /// </summary>
        /// <returns></returns>
        public AnimationModifierSettings GetModifierSettings();
        
        /// <summary>
        /// Standard game thread update.
        /// </summary>
        /// <param name="playable">Playable to update.</param>
        /// <param name="weight">General feature weight.</param>
        public void UpdateJobData(AnimationScriptPlayable playable, float weight);
        
        /// <summary>
        /// Called after the pose is finalized.
        /// </summary>
        public void LateUpdate();
        
        /// <summary>
        /// Destroys this job and disposes its data.
        /// </summary>
        public void Dispose();
        
        /// <summary>
        /// Draws the modifier's Gizmos.
        /// </summary>
        public void OnDrawGizmos();
    }

# Modify Bone | Character Animation System Docs

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/modify-bone#overview)

Overview


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Modify Bone** directly changes bone position, rotation, or scale.

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252F2XFUvskxTaBQkATEVcvc%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D686cc6e8-ecd5-4d48-82b8-da426a3ea2bf&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ce616f9a&sv=2)

Modify Bone.

*   **Bone To Modify** is the bone that will be modified.
    
*   **Position** is a Vector3 position property. It is possible to bind any Vector3 value to this property.
    
*   **Rotation** is a Quaternion rotation property. It is possible to bind any Quaternion value to this property.
    
*   **Scale** is a Vector3 scale property. It is possible to bind any Vector3 value to this property.
    
*   **Translation**/**Rotation Space**: Space to apply the position offset in.
    
*   **Translation**/**Rotation**/**Scale Mode**: Whether to ignore, add, or replace the current transform.
    

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/modify-bone#use-cases)

Use-cases


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This feature is used to modify a bone's transform at runtime. It's possible to bind offset values from external components (e.g., character controller) to drive the procedural animation logic.

[PreviousCopy Bonechevron-left](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/copy-bone)
[NextModify Bone Chainchevron-right](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/modify-bone-chain)

Last updated 3 months ago

*   [Overview](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/modify-bone#overview)
    
*   [Use-cases](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/modify-bone#use-cases)

# Foot IK | Character Animation System Docs

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/foot-ik#overview)

Overview


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Foot IK** is a simple modifier that corrects feet and pelvis position.

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FshBexQrxOZ1AIhbONj4n%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D57f2dfa4-0102-4137-8c63-ed121d71b931&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a6b68c96&sv=2)

Foot IK modifier.

*   **Layer Mask**: What layers to detect during a collision check.
    
*   **Pelvis**: Pelvis or a hip bone.
    
*   **Right Foot**: Right foot IK target.
    
*   **Left Foot**: Left foot IK target.
    
*   **Foot Height**: Height of the foot.
    
*   **Foot Radius**: Approximate radius of the foot.
    
*   **Ray Offset**: Vertical raycast offset.
    
*   **Interp Speed**: Smoothing speed. If set to 0, no smoothing will be applied.
    

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/foot-ik#use-cases)

Use-cases


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This modifier is used in combination with Two-Bone IKs for character legs. It is typically placed before the IK modifiers:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FNfDJTUURcO2vCUMLv3O9%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd6bfe328-96e2-4351-aa41-7435194aa0dd&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=aeb5f462&sv=2)

Procedural modifiers order.

[PreviousLook Modifierchevron-left](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/look-modifier)
[NextTwo Bone IKchevron-right](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/two-bone-ik)

Last updated 1 month ago

*   [Overview](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/foot-ik#overview)
    
*   [Use-cases](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/foot-ik#use-cases)

# Character Camera | Character Animation System Docs

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/character-camera#overview)

Overview


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Character Animation System** features a simple camera component that supports:

*   First- and third-person views.
    
*   Camera stabilization in first-person mode.
    
*   Camera shakes.
    
*   Smooth FOV updates.
    

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252F3wAL4VcLdaJuEYsJRJJI%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbb462ab3-bc26-4f06-8c52-8b05dd7fd4fa&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f2919a45&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/character-camera#inputs)

Inputs

> Input properties to control the camera.

*   **Yaw** and **Pitch Input** — horizontal and vertical input values.
    
*   **Is Aiming** — whether player is aiming.
    
*   **Is Crouching** — whether player is crouching or standing.
    
*   **Is First Person** — defines current view mode.
    
*   **Use Right Shoulder** — defines anchor shoulder.
    
*   **View Smoothing** — interpolation speed.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/character-camera#transforms)

Transforms

> Source transforms.

*   **First Person Socket** — camera will follow this transform when in first-person.
    
*   **Camera Animation Source** — animated transform that will be used to animate camera.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/character-camera#offsets)

Offsets

> Camera offsets for different situations.

Camera offsets are represented as struct properties:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FdBL6hb2NGu9h6VrUA1Wm%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dec32edaf-5d94-4a4b-acc0-dc1211c056ab&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b2b50385&sv=2)

*   Offset — position offset relative to the pivot point.
    
*   Pivot — pivot point offset relative to the origin.
    

circle-check

**Tip**: Character Camera uses player transform as origin

#### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/character-camera#camera-collision)

Camera Collision

> Tracing properties to avoid camera clipping with obstacles.

*   **Trace Radius** — sphere trace radius.
    
*   **Trace Interp Speed** — camera smoothing speed when adjusting for collision.
    
*   **Trace Mask** — what collision layers will be used.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/character-camera#fov)

FOV

Use this method to update target field-of-view:

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/character-camera#camera-shakes)

Camera Shakes


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Shakes** are fire-and-forget type of motions that can are played at runtime to simulate hits or recoil:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FLXvh7MJ9Zs7GpmZmDKsd%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd94a3ed8-f461-4c78-840f-11b4d6e1b685&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=df451705&sv=2)

*   **X** — rotation motion around X axis.
    
*   **Y** — rotation motion around Y axis.
    
*   **Z** — rotation motion around Z axis.
    
*   **Pitch**, **Yaw Roll** — Vector4 shake value range.
    
*   **Play Rate** — playback speed multiplier.
    
*   **Smooth Speed** — interpolation speed.
    

circle-info

**Tip**: A shake value is computed as a random between `Mathf.Random(ragne.x, range.y)` and `Mathf.Random(range.z, range.w)`.

Use this function to play camera shakes from code:

[PreviousAnimationschevron-left](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/example-content/animations)
[NextQuickstartchevron-right](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/fps-addon/quickstart)

Last updated 3 months ago

*   [Overview](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/character-camera#overview)
    
*   [FOV](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/character-camera#fov)
    
*   [Camera Shakes](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/character-camera#camera-shakes)
    

CharacterCamera.cs

Copy

    // interpSpeed controls how fast to reach the new field-of-view.
    public virtual void UpdateTargetFOV(float newFov, float interpSpeed = 0f)

CharacterCamera.cs

Copy

    public virtual void PlayCameraShake(CharacterCameraShake newShake)

# Look Modifier | Character Animation System Docs

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/look-modifier#overview)

Overview


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Look Modifier** is commonly used to apply spine rotation and leaning effects. This is essential to make the character look around without Blend Trees.

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FtADX1HgfL5DBdCD4qnNv%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcb0c8cf4-79fd-4129-9265-67622578ff39&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b548ef05&sv=2)

Look Modifier.

*   **Pitch Input**: pitch or look-up angle in degrees.
    
*   **Yaw Input**: yaw or look-right-left angle in degrees.
    
*   **Use Yaw As Delta**: whether to accumulate yaw input every frame.
    
*   **Use Yaw Turn Angle**: whether to use the turn-in-place angle. Set this to true if is used.
    
*   **Roll Input**: roll or leaning angle in degrees.
    
*   **Pitch**/**Yaw**/**Roll Offset Elements**: bones that will be affected by rotation.
    

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/look-modifier#use-cases)

Use-cases


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Look Modifier** is generally used for any effects that require distributed spine rotation. It is quite common to bind player input values from the gameplay code to control rotation:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FGIRMNogoXdOxGiZdGIYE%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D49d32a4e-fc73-45c9-a965-e9750f08a38a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a645f6e4&sv=2)

Using character controller value to drive the pitch input.

By default, **Yaw Input** is a world rotation value, which means you can bind the player's rotation directly to this property:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FIEuMIIdGaFHBUtvOINdL%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5eef6e6c-dcda-49ca-bd89-d04b4b57b9cd&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b03a9c33&sv=2)

How to Look using player's global aiming rotation.

If there isn't a global rotation value, it is recommended to use the player's horizontal delta input instead:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FEwvJ8NA2WM3MMzESjA2P%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D447a038e-df80-44e1-b825-e2fc061bff31&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bc9b1cda&sv=2)

How to Look using player's delta horizontal/yaw input.

circle-check

**Tip**: using the player's delta input is easy to implement, but it doesn't give that much control as global rotation. For example, if we were to add look smoothing, we would use the global rotation variable instead.

Look angles are automatically adjusted to match the 90-degree target:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252F3tqQyGf7qizGC3DMJtzF%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc7ce5449-e631-47c4-90e1-8add724eaca0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=73635ec7&sv=2)

Auto-angle distribution.

circle-check

**Tip**: Just type in the value, and the system will automatically compute the right angles for the rest of the list!

[PreviousModify Bone Chainchevron-left](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/modify-bone-chain)
[NextFoot IKchevron-right](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/foot-ik)

Last updated 4 months ago

*   [Overview](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/look-modifier#overview)
    
*   [Use-cases](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/look-modifier#use-cases)

# Two Bone IK | Character Animation System Docs

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/two-bone-ik#overview)

Overview


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Two Bone IK** attaches a limb, usually an arm or leg, to a world-space target or another bone.

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252Fp8ennUL3XiYSVvvMM1uH%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D68971d54-e599-406f-82d5-3a7dc3fd26ba&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=80194726&sv=2)

*   **Tip**: This bone will be aligned with a target. Usually, it is a hand or a foot.
    
*   **Target**: A bone to reach. It can be an IK bone or a custom Game Object in the hierarchy.
    
*   **Use World Target**: Whether to use world position and rotation as a target.
    
*   **IK Target Transform**: World-space target transform.
    
*   **Pole Target**: A pole/hint bone, which is typically an elbow or a knee.
    

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/two-bone-ik#use-cases)

Use-cases


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Two-Bone IK** is generally used in combination with other modifiers, like Foot or Step IK. It is also used to attach hands to props, like barrel or a lever.

#### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/two-bone-ik#ik-setup)

IK Setup

Most Two-Bone IK setups rely on proxy, empty Game Objects that work as IK bones:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FP8QJa0nFZiZg4WRknMBA%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df98c6b6f-515a-4fa3-ab44-1cbee0376b9e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=14fd1fca&sv=2)

IK Bones.

In Procedural Animation Settings, poses are copied from real (e.g., right hand or left foot) to IK bones using Copy Bone Modifiers:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FIPl5KPTCRwueRO8qGbz9%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D97d585c9-dc52-40e5-b826-25baa6a2d397&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=53663741&sv=2)

Copy right foot example.

Then, procedural logic is applied (e.g., Foot and Step IK):

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FQh2POFL0MXC8elBCVM97%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D526544fd-cac8-457f-918b-9a1c54553d5f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d925554c&sv=2)

IK Setup.

Finally, Two Bone IK modifiers are applied to animate hands or feet based on their targets.

Thanks to this workflow, it's possible to cache hands or feet animation, and then alter it procedurally without loosing the original character pose.

[PreviousFoot IKchevron-left](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/foot-ik)
[NextFull-body IKchevron-right](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/full-body-ik)

Last updated 1 month ago

*   [Overview](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/two-bone-ik#overview)
    
*   [Use-cases](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/two-bone-ik#use-cases)

# Example Content | Character Animation System Docs

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/example-content#overview)

Overview


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Character Animation System** comes with a free example demo package that includes animations, items, prefabs and scripts. Follow this guide to install the demo: [Install Demo Content](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/quickstart/introduction-to-cas/install-demo-content)
.

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FXts0fqnU8NsZMjUxlGm4%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddeeec510-c2c3-457e-8926-11148174430c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8bc732f3&sv=2)

CAS Demo folder.

*   **Animation** includes clips and animator controllers used in the demo, including Humanoid and Generic versions.
    
*   **CAS** contains Character, Procedural Animation Settings and Animation Assets.
    
*   **Climbing** includes data assets used for parkour.
    
*   **Interactions** contains data assets and settings used in interactions (e.g., pulling a lever).
    
*   **Meshes** includes all custom prop meshes used in the demo (e.g., torch, axe, etc.).
    
*   **Prefabs** contains item and character prefabs.
    

**Input\_CAS** is the main input asset used in the demo content. It defines general (like move, look or jump) and item-specific actions (e.g., aim or use item).

[🔹Example Controllerchevron-right](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/example-content/example-controller)
[🔹Itemschevron-right](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/example-content/items)
[🔸Animationschevron-right](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/example-content/animations)

[PreviousCharacter Skeletonchevron-left](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/character-skeleton)

# Items | Character Animation System Docs

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/example-content/items#overview)

Overview


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Cas Prop** is a component attached to all items wielded by the character:

*   **Torch**
    
*   **Barrel**
    
*   **Axe**
    
*   **Gun**
    

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FsuAcPwSlPXuH2JoZMlxo%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dffda1846-74c9-4ad2-a9ee-3a3c9e29ecbb&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a97f0df0&sv=2)

Cas Prop.

*   **Animation Settings** — [CAS](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/character-animation-component#character-animation-settings)
     asset for this item.
    
*   **Right** and **Left Hand Target** — IK targets for hands. These transforms are bound directly to the [Two Bone IK](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/two-bone-ik)
     modifiers.
    

All items reside in the character prefab:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FgkJhS3reZYPqejS2sFXH%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8d715520-16f9-4602-a346-a5e47ecd6efb&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ad3097d0&sv=2)

Torch, Axe and Gun prefabs are attached to the right hand. When the game starts, the [Character Example Controller](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/example-content/example-controller)
 will try to find all items and equip the first one.

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/example-content/items#api-reference)

API Reference


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[PreviousExample Controllerchevron-left](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/example-content/example-controller)
[NextAnimationschevron-right](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/example-content/animations)

Last updated 3 months ago

*   [Overview](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/example-content/items#overview)
    
*   [API Reference](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/example-content/items#api-reference)
    

CasProp.cs

Copy

    // Called when left-mouse button is pressed.
    public virtual void UseItem()
    {
    }
    
    // Called when left-mouse button is released.
    public virtual void StopUsingItem()
    {
    }
    
    // Called when this item becomes active.
    public virtual void OnEquipped()
    {
    }
    
    // Called when this item is holstered.
    public virtual float OnUnEquipped()
    {
        return 0f;
    }
    
    // Called when aiming input is updated.
    public virtual void OnAim(bool isAiming)
    {
    }
    
    // Called to update item's visibility.
    public virtual void SetVisibility(bool isVisible)
    {
        gameObject.SetActive(isVisible);
    }

# Full-body IK | Character Animation System Docs

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/full-body-ik#overview)

Overview


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FCcSJdJAW9nIZD4mMikE5%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D26763373-9d51-4fce-b63f-8a9c7cf3af23&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3146a2a1&sv=2)

This modifier has the same exact purpose as [Two Bone IK](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/two-bone-ik)
, the only difference is that it applies IK for arms and legs at the same time. Arms and legs have the same set of parameters:

*   **Tip** is the hand or foot bone.
    
*   **Target** is the IK target bone (e.g., IK hand\_r or IK foot\_l).
    
*   **Pole Target** is the hint or knee bone.
    
*   **Weight** controls the IK influence.
    
*   **Pole Weight** is the elbow/knee influence.
    

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/full-body-ik#use-cases)

Use-cases


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This modifier is useful when you don't want to have multiple Two Bone IK features in procedural settings. It also gives you a complete control over all IK bone chains with [Weight Overrides](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers#weight-overrides)
.

[PreviousTwo Bone IKchevron-left](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/two-bone-ik)
[NextStep Modifierchevron-right](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/step-modifier)

Last updated 1 month ago

*   [Overview](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/full-body-ik#overview)
    
*   [Use-cases](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/full-body-ik#use-cases)

# Property Bindings | Character Animation System Docs

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/property-bindings#overview)

Overview


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Property Bindings** is a system for binding values in the editor. CAS uses it to link gameplay code (e.g., character controllers) with the animation system (Procedural Animation and Layered Blending).

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FfSi4ZHc4pVUCTTNaQ37k%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc75db421-d91e-45c1-a5dc-7bd10ccfad30&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=665df9f8&sv=2)

Example of a property binding.

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/property-bindings#editor)

Editor


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When pressing the "**+**" icon, a property binding will try to search for potential bindable public fields, properties, and methods. Here is what happens on the low level:

1.  Get a GameObject context — it is typically a player prefab reference, provided by the interface.
    
2.  Iterate over all components and look for public fields, properties, and methods that return the desired type.
    
3.  Create a dropdown menu with potential bindables.
    
4.  Once a bindable is selected, the binding's path and component type will be updated.
    

To get a GameObject context, Property Bindings rely on the IBindableContext interface:

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/property-bindings#initialization)

Initialization


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Property Bindings needs to be manually built, which typically happens when the game starts:

circle-check

**Tip**: The process of building bindings can be slow; it is highly recommended to build them only once when the game starts!

In some cases, it is important to create a safe copy of a property:

This can be useful when one binding is used with different instances. For example, if we bind a player-controlled offset to the animation system, we must ensure that each instance of our player has separate control over that bound property.

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/property-bindings#getting-a-value)

Getting a value


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`BindableProperty.GetValue()` is used to return the current value of a bound property.

circle-check

**Tip**: Property Bindings have a built-in null check for reference types, which makes it safe to use at runtime, even if one of the references is null.

`BindableProperty.SetDefaultValue(T value)` is used to update the default value of the property. The default value is only used when:

*   A property wasn't initialized successfully.
    
*   One of the references is null.
    

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/property-bindings#updating-context)

Updating context


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When a binding is built during initialization, on the low level, it creates a function that takes a MonoBehaviour component as a parameter. It is possible to change the context for a property at runtime:

circle-check

**Tip**: This is useful when we don't want to rebuild the property (because it's too expensive), but instead can change the target component to extract the bound value from.

[PreviousState Behaviourschevron-left](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/state-behaviours)
[NextCharacter Skeletonchevron-right](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/character-skeleton)

Last updated 3 months ago

*   [Overview](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/property-bindings#overview)
    
*   [Editor](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/property-bindings#editor)
    
*   [Initialization](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/property-bindings#initialization)
    
*   [Getting a value](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/property-bindings#getting-a-value)
    
*   [Updating context](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/property-bindings#updating-context)
    

Copy

    public interface IBindableContext
    {
        public GameObject GetContext();
    }

ModifyBoneSettings.cs

Copy

    public override void InitializeOnLoad()
    {
        base.InitializeOnLoad();
                
        position.Initialize(characterPrefab);
        rotation.Initialize(characterPrefab);
        scale.Initialize(characterPrefab);
    }

ModifyBoneJob.cs

Copy

    _position = _modifierSettings.position.CreateProperty(_jobData.animator.gameObject);
    _rotation = _modifierSettings.rotation.CreateProperty(_jobData.animator.gameObject);
    _scale = _modifierSettings.scale.CreateProperty(_jobData.animator.gameObject);

Copy

    BindableProperty.UpdateContext(GameObject context)

# Copy Bone | Character Animation System Docs

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/copy-bone#overview)

Overview


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Copy Bone** copies data from one bone to another:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FaSW4YZDHL24ZUZWrSkeT%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D65f780ce-ac90-4e8d-a935-63269f417da6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=43d626ad&sv=2)

*   **Copy From** is the bone to copy data from.
    
*   **Copy To** is the bone to copy data to.
    
*   **Copy Mode** defines how the pose will be copied:
    
    *   (Default) **Replace** will replace the target transform.
        
    *   **Add** will accumulate the target transform.
        
    
*   **Copy Position** controls whether to copy position.
    
*   **Copy Rotation** controls whether to copy rotation
    
*   **Copy Position** controls whether to copy scale.
    

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/copy-bone#use-cases)

Use-cases


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This modifier is mostly useful for IK bones. For example, here is a setup that's used in the CAS Demo:

1.  Copy data from real bones to IK (e.g., from right hand to IK hand\_r).
    
2.  Animate the IK target (e.g., add translation to IK hand\_r).
    
3.  Apply IK (e.g., Two Bone IK for the right arm).
    

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FcDPVLLx8hJkKS3T0l4jM%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4a82d1ac-bb09-4176-8f26-bc1e222569ee&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=37f6ac0f&sv=2)

Simple IK setup example.

[PreviousAnimation Modifierschevron-left](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers)
[NextModify Bonechevron-right](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/modify-bone)

Last updated 3 months ago

*   [Overview](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/copy-bone#overview)
    
*   [Use-cases](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/copy-bone#use-cases)

# Pivot Modifier | Character Animation System Docs

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/pivot-modifier#overview)

Overview


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Pivot Modifier** applies spine rotation and pelvis translation when starting or stopping moving. It also adds leaning rotation towards the velocity.

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FUTkYhoIedeAMBB651CIU%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D168c0e59-cdf6-4726-a6e5-455d2a68ce27&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a681b26f&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/pivot-modifier#bone-references)

Bone References

> These properties define what bones will be affected by this modifier.

*   **Pelvis** is the pelvis or hip bone.
    
*   **Spine Bones** is the bone chain that will be affected by the leaning rotation.
    

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FFLoLgvzLmasKtBvO50Ut%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbd375e4c-c632-4abf-abb9-2ee47abaa030&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=89759571&sv=2)

Spine bones example.

#### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/pivot-modifier#animation)

Animation

> These properties define the leaning motion.

*   **Rotation Curve** is the animation for spine bones.
    
*   **Translation Curve** is the animation for pelvis.
    
*   Rotation and Position Smoothing control the interpolation speed for rotation/translation.
    
*   Playback Speed is the animation speed multiplier.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/pivot-modifier#leaning)

Leaning

> These properties control the leaning rotation.

*   **Max Lean Angle** is the max rotation angle in degrees.
    
*   **Lean Intensity** controls how strong the leaning rotation will be.
    

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/pivot-modifier#use-cases)

Use-cases


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This modifier can be used to add dynamic leaning rotation effects when moving around. The default settings are already adjusted to work with any character, except for spine bones:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FFLoLgvzLmasKtBvO50Ut%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbd375e4c-c632-4abf-abb9-2ee47abaa030&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=89759571&sv=2)

It's recommended to assign bones here.

[PreviousStep Modifierchevron-left](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/step-modifier)
[NextAim Atchevron-right](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/aim-at)

Last updated 1 month ago

*   [Overview](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/pivot-modifier#overview)
    
*   [Use-cases](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/pivot-modifier#use-cases)
