# Animations | Character Animation System Docs

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/example-content/animations#animator-controller)

Animator Controller


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The base animator controller is included in the CAS package:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FpvlcxzZvN4pLfhj3QkhF%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddd8b53aa-f4f7-4746-a929-4580083324fa&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bf4aab60&sv=2)

Base controller.

It's supposed to be used as a template, as it only contains empty animation states — placeholders that can be overriddent with Override Animator Controller feature.

**Generic** and **Humanoid** versions can be found in **Assets ▸ CAS Demo ▸ Animations ▸ Generic or Humanoid.**

circle-info

**Note**: Generic animations are only compatible with the Kinemation Mannequin (**KINEMATION ▸ Shared ▸ Character**).

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FKxMmHFA0VMqzspZGCC05%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D598225cc-e2d8-4024-8479-6a09ce3d3235&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3fe2b400&sv=2)

Animation Layers.

The controller consists of 5 main animation layers.

#### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/example-content/animations#curves)

Curves

This layer sets curve blending properties to default values:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FXm3JdMuw1k1EPs15SGxx%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddaca9a7a-84c3-4613-8380-99246508397a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ccf239ee&sv=2)

It contains only a single state — **Curves\_Default**. This Animation Clip only contains bindings to the blending float parameters:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FOUwWuCN9s0misuIkmIgh%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc7549827-a5c1-4904-a5da-d93d7a215f53&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2688c8bd&sv=2)

It's very important to zero all parameters to avoid situations when blending properties have values from previous frames. If not zeroed, blending values might cause jittering issues.

#### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/example-content/animations#stance)

Stance

This layer blends between standing and crouching states.

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FS1aoZcY4KAYuOl1liAJc%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dad535789-f28d-4d89-8d5a-f1424f773353&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d6a51e54&sv=2)

Stances.

These are empty states, which are only used to animate the **CrouchWeight** value using the [**SetFloat**](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/state-behaviours#set-float)
 feature.

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FvY9hKUGOqK7r1gkbVeRv%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D212508be-93ac-4a56-8cc2-171bb2815a87&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b9ee38d8&sv=2)

circle-info

**Tip**: The **CrouchWeight** is an Animator float parameter that is used to blend between standing and crouched character movement.

#### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/example-content/animations#locomotion)

Locomotion

This layer applies full-body animations, like idle, jogging, sprinting and jumping.

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252F1F7LbON3ZA9J1K4x8cjU%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc8fc1efc-3bcb-4afd-b3b3-417e689fc446&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e0edb5e2&sv=2)

Locomotion.

**Grounded** is a blend tree that blends between different stance and movement animations.

#### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/example-content/animations#turn-in-place)

Turn In Place

This layer triggered procedural steps when turning left or right.

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252F9ExtpHbRZi9il5FCDvnN%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7c850f56-cdbb-471e-8ee6-97ffdb65d698&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2c1462c&sv=2)

Turn in place states.

**TurnRight** and **TurnLeft** are empty states by default. It's possible to override them with turning animations. Instead, CAS uses [**Play Step**](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/state-behaviours#play-step)
 behaviours to play procedural steps when turning:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FbqeXJF5jEw8x7VGy3g7X%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2d279402-0315-44e0-9f90-47fe67828fa1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b6815605&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/example-content/animations#interactions)

Interactions

This last layer is reserved for full-body interaction animations, like climbing or pulling a lever:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FvbInBO0MItO6nL5j9gAf%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddf109767-3b6c-40bc-8127-673baf0c8708&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=89835a8&sv=2)

Interaction states.

The default state is empty, because all interaction clips are triggered from code using the CrossFade function. Interactions automatically blend out to the empty state upon completion.

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FJT4zC4xi7Rqy0C0NIkoL%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0862a990-da39-4c33-a0aa-1c16aba1cf1c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5aefe70b&sv=2)

Interaction transition parameters.

[PreviousItemschevron-left](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/example-content/items)
[NextCharacter Camerachevron-right](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/character-camera)

# Example Controller | Character Animation System Docs

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/example-content/example-controller#overview)

Overview


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Character Example Controller** handles player movement and input actions, such as:

*   Crouch, Sprint and Jump
    
*   Look and leaning
    
*   Items equip, use and unequip
    
*   Climbing and vaulting
    

To function properly, it requires Character Controller and Player Input components:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252F6Q1pWRCvTjHdFo2EHvjU%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd22479a8-847c-41a8-8fa2-d7c50e4a1dcf&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4d68edc3&sv=2)

Character Controller and Player Inputs.

### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/example-content/example-controller#update-flow)

Update Flow

When the game starts, the example controller will try to find **CasProp** components in the hierarchy — items like torch, axe or barrel — and equip the first found item. It supposses that items are added directly to the character (for example, parented to the right hand).

On `Update()`, it processes character speed, rotation and movement based on the input values.

This component receives messages from the **Player Input** to implement custom actions:

*   **OnInteract()** — tries to start an interaction.
    
*   **OnSprint()** — tries to start sprinting.
    
*   **OnCrouch()** — toggles current crouching state.
    
*   **OnLook(InputValue value)** — accumulates delta look values.
    
*   **OnJump()** — tries to jump.
    
*   **OnMove(InputValue value)** — updates player Vector2 input direction.
    
*   **OnAim(InputValue value)** — updates camera and active item aiming status.
    
*   **OnTogglePerspective()** — toggles first- and third-person views.
    
*   **OnChangeShoulder()** — toggles between right and left shoulder views.
    
*   **OnLean(InputValue value)** — updates current leaning angle.
    

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/example-content/example-controller#properties)

Properties


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/example-content/example-controller#controller)

Controller

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252Fs5mZaQhTu64K63ZUBpDr%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbb1872c3-14e9-4503-8b4b-6bcfead20424&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3ca03236&sv=2)

Character Example Controller.

*   **Time Scale** — active time scale value.
    
*   **Mouse Sensitivity** — look input sensitivity multiplier.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/example-content/example-controller#standing)

Standing

> Standing movement properties.

*   **Acceleration** — how fast player should accelerate.
    
*   **Deceleration** — how fast player should decelerate.
    
*   **Walk Speed** — normal speed when walking.
    
*   **Sprint Speed** — normal speed when sprinting.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/example-content/example-controller#crouching)

Crouching

*   **Crouch Walk Speed** — walking speed when crouched.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/example-content/example-controller#in-air)

In Air

> In air parameters.

*   **Jump Height** — how far should the character jump.
    
*   **Fall Delay** — time ungrounded before entering the in air state.
    
*   **Gravity** — how strong is the force pulling player back to the ground.
    
*   **Max Fall Velocity** — this will clamp max fall speed.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/example-content/example-controller#view)

View

> Perspective and rotation mode.

*   **Is First Person** — controls active perspective.
    
*   **Orient Rotation To Movement** — aligns rotation with the movement vector. This feature only in third-person mode.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/example-content/example-controller#animation)

Animation

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FJFqFwv8NIHKVGsiTHq9S%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D846767a3-ba5f-4f4d-aea5-60fc83d74878&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2ebe713&sv=2)

*   **Lean Angle** — max leaning angle.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/example-content/example-controller#steps)

Steps

> [Procedural steps](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/step-modifier)
>  played to avoid feet sliding.

*   **Steps Crouch**/**Uncrouch** — played when player is crouching or uncrouching.
    
*   **Step In Place** — played when player is changing items.
    
*   **Start**/**Stop Moving** — played during movement transitions.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/example-content/example-controller#smoothing)

Smoothing

> Animation smoothing based on the target velocity (acceleration, deceleration).

*   **Animator Standing** — applied when standing.
    
*   **Animator Crouching** — applied when crouching.

# Step Modifier | Character Animation System Docs

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/step-modifier#overview)

Overview


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Step Modifier** creates procedural steps to avoid feet sliding when changing animation states (e.g., standing to crouching).

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252F0aKbhfqtQGBpryK91tUu%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da01c49eb-236d-45f2-8188-db5a5687e7ac&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b9d0dc9e&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/step-modifier#bone-references)

Bone References

> Here you will find bone references to assign.

*   **Pelvis** is the character pelvis or hip bone.
    
*   **Right** and **Left Foot IK Target**: is the IK bone for the right or left foot. It's usually set to IK foot\_r or IK foot\_l.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/step-modifier#ground-alignment)

Ground Alignment

> Here you will find settings for snapping feet to the ground.

*   **Right Foot** is the character right foot bone (not an IK).
    
*   **Left Foot** is the character left foot bone (not an IK).
    
*   **Leg Stretch Factor** fine-tunes how aggressively the system detects and corrects leg stretching. Higher values increase the likelihood that a leg will be classified as “stretched” and have its length adjusted accordingly.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/step-modifier#step-motion)

Step Motion

> Here you will find animation curves for feet and pelvis.

*   **Lead Foot Motion** is the position animation for the leading foot (the one making a step first).
    
*   **Follow Foot Motion** is the position animation for the following foot (the one making a step after the leading one).
    
*   **Pelvis Motion** is the position animation for pelvis.
    

circle-info

**Note**: The Animation Curve values must at end zero for all motions.

*   **Lead**, **Follow Foot** and **Pelvis Scale** are values that will scale each motion per-axis. For example, the X component will scale the X axis.
    
*   **Play Rate** is the speed multiplier for this step motion.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/step-modifier#stride-settings)

Stride Settings

> Here you will properties that define the procedural step.

*   **Animated Lead Foot** defines the leading foot for this step. A leading foot is the one making a step first.
    
*   **Force Lead Foot** controls if the step must always start with a leading foot. If disabled, the leading foot will be determined based on the velocity vector.
    
*   **Max Allowed Strength** defines the max allowed step length. If exceeded, feet will be moved in the movement direction to avoid stretching.
    
*   **Max Allowed Offset Angle** defines the max allowed character rotation to avoid leg twisting. If exceeded, feet will be rotated around pelvis to compensate the rotation.
    
*   **Step Cooldown Rate** is the time in seconds needed to pass before making the next step.
    

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/step-modifier#use-cases)

Use-cases


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Step Modifier** can be used for any situation to replace feet sliding with a nice procedural step. Here are most popular applications:

1.  Movement stop or start transitions.
    
2.  New stance transition (e.g., going from rifle to sword, or from standing to crouching).
    
3.  Turning in place.
    

circle-check

**Tip**: CAS comes with example Step presets, these can be found in KINEMATION/CharacterAnimationSystem/Examples/Steps/.

### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/step-modifier#recommended-settings)

Recommended settings

To get best results, make sure that:

1.  **MaxAllowedStride** is set to ~0.3-0.4 to avoid character legs being strecthed. Setting this to a too small number will result in abrupt, unnatural steps.
    
2.  **MaxAllowedOffsetAngle** is set to ~45 degrees to avoid legs being twisted.
    
3.  **StepCooldownRate** is set to ~0.3-0.4s to handle player input-spamming situations.
    
4.  **Force Lead Foot** can be used for specific cases, like turning in place — we only want to turn right with the right foot, and vice versa.
    
5.  All animation curves start at zero for a seamless transition.
    

These settings might differ from one character model to another, so it's fine to experiment and find what works best for your character.

### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/step-modifier#how-to-play-steps)

How to play steps

Steps can be played at runtime using by updating the animation modifier:

It's possible to play steps when a transition is entering or exiting a state in the Animator:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252F8G7pu7sq4cRHxkiRVLCx%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D79c59a18-2a2a-4d9a-8fa9-40daa3ab9332&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fa41ceb&sv=2)

Syncing steps with animation states.

This feature is used in the CAS Demo to play steps when turning in place or finishing climbing.

[PreviousFull-body IKchevron-left](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/full-body-ik)
[NextPivot Modifierchevron-right](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/pivot-modifier)

Last updated 1 month ago

*   [Overview](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/step-modifier#overview)
    
*   [Use-cases](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/step-modifier#use-cases)
    
*   [Recommended settings](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/step-modifier#recommended-settings)
    
*   [How to play steps](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/step-modifier#how-to-play-steps)
    

YourComponent.cs

Copy

    private ProceduralAnimationComponent _proceduralAnimation;
    private StepModifierSettings _yourStepModifier;
    
    private void YourMethod()
    {
        _proceduralAnimation.UpdateAnimationModifier(_yourStepModifier);
    }

# FPS Setup | Character Animation System Docs

circle-exclamation

**Tip:** If you’re new to CAS, use the **KINEMATION/Shared/Character** humanoid model.

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/fps-addon/quickstart/fps-setup#character)

Character


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Add your character to the scene, right-click on it and select "KINEMATION/Setup CAS":

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252F62y6qBtnCu56PQIxgEAc%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De90b0a12-2ce2-4edc-aeb4-80e5120f4db9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f6f5a1f2&sv=2)

Select the **FPS** preset:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FoR5sUvXNuOehezKiLfjf%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D49ea2132-cc88-4b58-9f44-317e44748008&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=809c4993&sv=2)

FPS preset.

circle-info

**Note**: It will only show up if the demo content is installed.

Then, follow the setup steps:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FrgbJTmvdAUib6UPQhBY3%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D439d6197-44d8-4530-9f32-8ca366754d4c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=993a17f3&sv=2)

FPS Preset.

#### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/fps-addon/quickstart/fps-setup#id-1.-skeleton-type)

1\. Skeleton Type

Select the type of your character model skeleton:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FqWLlU15CHhEFDU1b0Vs3%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8b79b3d4-f1e7-4f84-bd05-1b690bad557b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=706de443&sv=2)

Select your skeleton type.

CAS supports most popular model types:

*   Unreal Mannequin (UE4&UE5).
    
*   Mixamo
    
*   Character Creator (CC4, CC5)
    
*   Synty
    

For other models, pick the "Default" option - CAS will try to find bones recursively.

#### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/fps-addon/quickstart/fps-setup#id-2.-animations)

2\. Animations

Next, we need to pick Animation Clips for our character:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252F3DZZDuFgjHCgHEa4cQYt%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6da06141-7672-4d24-b9a1-83ce6b3ec750&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3cab181&sv=2)

Assign Animation Clips.

**Base Pose** is your character standing idle animation. CAS uses it to compute additive motion in runtime.

**Overlay Pose** is your weapon idle animation. **Overlay Controller** reference can be left empty, we will add it in the next pages.

#### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/fps-addon/quickstart/fps-setup#id-3.-bones)

3\. Bones

Finally, we need to assign bone references, so CAS can create Procedural Animation Modifiers:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FeOXx8o0j9CTtmfM5ACfr%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De7abcd24-fb95-4078-9983-1ffc17876a82&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=12cc501b&sv=2)

Assign bone references.

By default, this window will prompt you to select a Weapon Bone - a special bone in the character skeleton that contains weapon movement. If your model doesn't have such a bone, you can skip this step and apply the preset.

Once all bones are assigned, you can press the "Apply Preset" button.

If something is missing, you will see a warning what bones should be assigned manually:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FE3fEKdzK1KvqpKfLoIJu%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D25fd813a-8147-4bed-ba59-7d4a3d81a9f4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f63dee37&sv=2)

Warning example.

#### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/fps-addon/quickstart/fps-setup#id-4.-assign-animator)

4\. Assign Animator

If your character is **Generic**, you will need to assign an Animator Controller:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FYtdrwEvqhem6pbSZnVTm%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D17532175-6126-4a0d-b8e7-c84a940a77af&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b3f778ef&sv=2)

Assign your Animator Controller here.

circle-info

**Tip**: Ensure that the selected animations and Animator are compatible with your skeleton! Generics will only work with Generic animations, and Humanoids - with Humanoid clips.

[PreviousFPS Demo Contentchevron-left](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/fps-addon/quickstart/fps-demo-content)
[NextSkeleton & IKchevron-right](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/fps-addon/quickstart/skeleton-and-ik)

# Attach Hand | Character Animation System Docs

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/fps-addon/modifiers/attach-hand#overview)

Overview


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This modifier is used to attach the left hand to the weapon:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FKN977F7WH1isyEqDdNbR%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfcd6697b-84d2-4a22-968c-3918ff59d2df&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fed2bb6a&sv=2)

*   **Default Hand Bone** is the default bone pose for the left hand. By default, it's set to IK hand\_l\_right.
    
*   **Ik Hand Bone** is left-hand IK bone. The default value is IK hand\_l.
    
*   **Ik Weapon Bone** is the IK weapon\_bone.
    
*   **Fingers** is a bone chain that includes left-hand bone fingers.
    
*   **Hand Pose** is an Animation Clip of the current grip pose.
    
*   **Attach Transform** is the transform the hand will be attached to.
    

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/fps-addon/modifiers/attach-hand#use-cases)

Use-cases


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Attach Hand modifier can be used to implement custom grip poses for attachments. Here's an example from the example demo content:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FlK9hhFUSozd09KvmpjRs%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De2640ef4-3093-40f6-8abc-2da08a1493fd&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9ed7aec&sv=2)

In this example, a weapon provides an animation pose and a target transform for the left hand.

circle-info

**Note**: If the target transform is **null**, then the **Default Hand Bone** (IK hand\_l\_right) will be used instead.

The **IK hand\_l\_right** is a dynamic bone that contains the idle left-hand pose relative to the right hand.

[PreviousFPS Copy Boneschevron-left](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/fps-addon/modifiers/fps-copy-bones)
[NextFPS Offsetchevron-right](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/fps-addon/modifiers/fps-offset)

Last updated 3 months ago

# Adding a Weapon | Character Animation System Docs

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/fps-addon/quickstart/adding-a-weapon#gun-prefab)

Gun Prefab


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Let's add an SMG to our character. We will use the demo **A\_W\_SMG** prefab and drag and drop it under the character's IK weapon\_bone GameObject.

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252Fng0KYxQfSvjD9LBc4ojD%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df4cec7ae-4668-4443-a81f-2da0cf8b5d3b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c55350b8&sv=2)

Locate this prefab.

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FmjGfLhGbIFLwvJoaM0s6%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5842df50-b808-4e48-ac4a-e7d573a2812f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ccf0cd7&sv=2)

Attach it to the gun bone.

Click on this prefab and find the Weapon component. Assign previously created CAS asset here:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FyGE6KGs7TrfxWzO6UfRb%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D13c6df82-0a9a-4291-a664-d63ae717d933&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8ac487a7&sv=2)

Assign the settings.

This links the overlay and procedural settings to this weapon, so when it’s equipped, CAS will use the correct animation data.

Now, let’s press Play and see how it looks in-game.

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/fps-addon/quickstart/adding-a-weapon#overlay-animator-controller)

Overlay Animator Controller


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you use a Humanoid or a different Generic character, it won't look great out of the box:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FmgnQ4q4IZImDB1V5WNtw%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddb6a0f08-167b-4a3d-9711-00fb57916ad6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6487e1a0&sv=2)

To fix this issue, go to **Create/Animation/Animation Override Controller**:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FjQ4khpw2fzIpGLiV6jXQ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Deb097cd5-8f28-422f-b0be-79ca29bc4976&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8801eca8&sv=2)

Use AC\_CAS\_FPS\_Character as Controller.

Here we need to assign:

*   **Idle\_Aim**: This is your weapon idle pose.
    
*   **Idle\_Rest**: This is a weapon pose when not aiming in third-person.
    
*   **Idle\_Rest\_Crouch**: Same as Idle\_Rest, but used only when crouching.
    

circle-check

**Tip**: CAS demo has example animations for Humanoid characters, you can find them in **CAS Demo/Animations/Generic**.

Assign this controller in CAS settings as **Overlay Animator**:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252Fmrvx4jQYQOcNBbvhWl2g%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2769c983-98e1-40f6-8852-623bb422fed2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6d08f652&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/fps-addon/quickstart/adding-a-weapon#weapon-pose)

Weapon Pose


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If your animations do not use a weapon bone, or your model is Humanoid — the weapon will follow the right hand by default:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FlhDcsThdJgw3ct0idlRH%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D75c0338b-d2c7-49db-955f-2f7d366077b3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2a739160&sv=2)

Weapon pose in first-person view.

Click the axis button in the **Procedural Animation** asset:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FaTkRbezfq2zt4JBIKJnr%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcd60f985-bdc7-4968-8d10-03c807020734&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5c477d25&sv=2)

Toggle this icon.

This will enable control Gizmos, which you can use to position the weapon in the editor:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FiGd2Qpa5XOQLQ9O3j9tM%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D30404034-af1a-4996-b765-f94b418d8778&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=40c5633b&sv=2)

Use translation and rotation controls.

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/fps-addon/quickstart/adding-a-weapon#fixing-left-hand)

Fixing Left Hand


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Select the SMG prefab, and locate attachment game objects:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FjzkbnEt5Bq1lKx2FhaRm%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De6bc33d7-1e29-4de7-89c7-5942d92fbf56&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8eeff944&sv=2)

Select grip attachmnets one by one.

Assign the animations compatible with your character in the **Grip Attachment** inspector:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FNYlhdE24c1BkO6kjqSEi%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9e5277d3-bcb0-4b27-adcb-ac623014c876&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=42f53df0&sv=2)

Assign the right clip here.

Once the correct clips have been assigned, the character left hand pose will look normal:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FI9uWcUb6IulwqqePmYW1%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D45824d88-ac56-4e41-9597-8c0e95cf4d37&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3046e0ea&sv=2)

Correct left hand position.

# Aim At | Character Animation System Docs

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/aim-at#overview)

Overview


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/aim-at#aim-at)

◻️ Aim At


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/aim-at#overview-1)

Overview

Aim At is an animation modifier that rotates selected bones so the character can **look at** (or **aim toward**) a target in **world space**.

You can align a single bone precisely (such as a head or weapon bone) and optionally add support bones to distribute the rotation through the body.

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FBC0AoeERgMru97GdI8Mc%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D348be08d-c304-4d50-8cc0-88dc1909dedd&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=77234bf&sv=2)

Aim At properties.

*   **Aim Bone**: The primary bone that must align to the target as accurately as possible (for example, a head or gun bone).
    
*   **Support Aim Bones**: Additional bones that also rotate toward the target to help carry the motion (for example, spine or neck bones).
    
*   **Forward Axis**: The local “forward” axis of the **Aim Bone** (the axis that should point at the target).
    
*   **Max Aim Distance**: Cancels aiming if the target exceeds this distance.
    
*   **Max Aim Pitch Angle**: Disables aiming if the required pitch rotation exceeds this limit.
    
*   **Max Aim Yaw Angle**: Disables aiming if the required yaw rotation exceeds this limit.
    
*   **Aim At Smoothing**: Interpolation speed for aiming; higher values converge faster.
    

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/aim-at#use-cases)

Use-cases


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Use Aim At to make NPCs (or player characters) look at or aim toward a point of interest in the game world. This modifier is typically driven by the **Aim At component**, which you add directly to the character.

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252F5HcKfaL9Ykr87wcojK9z%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Deb07613e-9851-41d9-8206-f40da33d71cd&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c358227e&sv=2)

Aim At component.

Add the **Aim At** component to your character, assign the target **Transform**, and toggle the feature in code as needed. You can also drive aiming by setting a target position directly at runtime.

### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/aim-at#recommended-settings)

Recommended Settings

#### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/aim-at#bones)

Bones

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FidKU8VEsgrW0oP8R8Kkl%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D405c0f0a-2149-4096-b67e-40a30fff8543&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7803b58b&sv=2)

Bone settings.

**Aim Bone** is the main bone that points at the target. This is commonly the head or weapon bone, but any bone can be used if it represents the direction you want to align.

**Support Aim Bones** are typically spine (and/or neck) bones. Use them to distribute rotation across the chain so the motion looks natural and does not hinge on a single joint.

#### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/aim-at#other)

Other

**Forward Axis** must match the local forward vector of your chosen **Aim Bone**. Before running the game, select the bone and identify which local axis represents “forward,” then enter that value.

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FQ6qLlVJIryZMmnuCTGiC%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3325de05-ef71-43d7-950e-cdcb8067a09e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e75ad1c7&sv=2)

In our example, the head forward axis is (0f, -1f, 0f).

circle-check

**Tip**: Example: if the head’s forward axis is `(0f, -1f, 0f)`, enter `(0f, -1f, 0f)` in **Forward Axis** so the Aim Bone rotates correctly toward the target.

**Max Aim Distance** limits the effective aiming range (default: **100 units**).

**Max Aim Pitch** and **Max Aim Yaw** constrain rotation. If the target would require rotation beyond these thresholds, aiming is cancelled/disabled.

**Aim At Smoothing** controls responsiveness. Higher values feel snappier; lower values feel more damped. A typical starting point is **8**, then adjust based on gameplay needs.

[PreviousPivot Modifierchevron-left](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/pivot-modifier)
[NextDynamic Boneschevron-right](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/dynamic-bones)

Last updated 1 month ago

*   [Overview](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/aim-at#overview)
    
*   [◻️ Aim At](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/aim-at#aim-at)
    
*   [Overview](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/aim-at#overview-1)
    
*   [Use-cases](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/aim-at#use-cases)
    
*   [Recommended Settings](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/animation-modifiers/aim-at#recommended-settings)
    

AimAtComponent.cs

Copy

    // Modify this public field at runtime.
    AimAtComponent.aimAtPosition

# FPS Copy Bones | Character Animation System Docs

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/fps-addon/modifiers/fps-copy-bones#overview)

Overview


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This modifier copies bone data to the IK bones.

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FvBpE0EXAjN7Jz2eNO4FL%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1f32b6df-2b57-439c-985b-0c9076502a49&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6be55bd2&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/fps-addon/modifiers/fps-copy-bones#copy-from)

Copy From

These are the bones that will provide the animation pose data.

*   Source Weapon Bone is usually the IK weapon\_bone\_r.
    
*   Source Right/Left Hand is a right or left hand bone.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/fps-addon/modifiers/fps-copy-bones#copy-to)

Copy To

These are the bones that will copy the animation pose from previous bones.

*   Ik Weapon Bone is the IK weapon\_bone, which represents the weapon animated transform.
    
*   Ik Weapon Bone Aim is the bone that contains the weapon idle pose, which is used for aiming.
    
*   Ik Hand Right/Left is an IK target bone for the right/left arm.
    

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/fps-addon/modifiers/fps-copy-bones#use-cases)

Use-cases


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This modifier lets you copy the animation poses from real bones to IK targets. This can be useful if there's a need to alter an existing animation without breaking the animation pose.

**FPS Copy Bones** is usually placed on top of all other modifiers in the settings:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252F4sETOBO4769RQUB7aEmX%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D61c96387-09aa-443b-9884-88c91edddc04&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=56516708&sv=2)

[PreviousModifierschevron-left](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/fps-addon/modifiers)
[NextAttach Handchevron-right](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/fps-addon/modifiers/attach-hand)

Last updated 3 months ago

*   [Overview](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/fps-addon/modifiers/fps-copy-bones#overview)

# Skeleton & IK | Character Animation System Docs

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/fps-addon/quickstart/skeleton-and-ik#overview)

Overview


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

After applying the preset, you will see these scriptable objects and prefabs creates in the current directory:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252F1UtlDU5SozMrKBjpJCMm%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D82c2f6d0-a352-4741-9124-653ed7921497&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=17f22432&sv=2)

Assets after the setup.

All these assets are briefly explained in [After Setup](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/quickstart/introduction-to-cas/after-setup)
.

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/fps-addon/quickstart/skeleton-and-ik#character-skeleton)

Character Skeleton


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

One of the created prefabs has a "Skeleton\_" prefix. This is a variant of your character model, which contains components such as:

*   **Character Animation**: Central component that manages other components.
    
*   **Layered Blending**: Blends your Animator with weapon Overlays.
    
*   **Procedural Animation**: Applies animation modifiers, like Sway or Ads.
    
*   **Character Skeleton**: Stored skeleton information.
    

The preset tool creates IK game objects that are used by procedural animation.

#### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/fps-addon/quickstart/skeleton-and-ik#ik-feet)

IK Feet

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FWpItIHzIMEflnLZCKuJs%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D748b24c4-7beb-497a-8109-b92f4530486e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=72eba2ee&sv=2)

**IK foot\_r** and **IK foot\_l** are used as IK targets for character legs. They are parented to the top bone in the hierarchy (e.g., root, armature, skeleton).

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FnlFl0LQSFb6ub26VCjRB%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df6b387df-8c74-411e-8fc9-4782d7349412&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3a51d803&sv=2)

Example of how bones are used in Procedural Animation Settings (PAs).

#### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/fps-addon/quickstart/skeleton-and-ik#ik-weapon-and-hands)

IK Weapon and Hands

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FdKPRpbUYGtLsibYOSFxh%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D746930b7-f3ae-4d6e-bf88-f367e91ca78f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b3419b9e&sv=2)

These bones are used to position the gun and hands with IK:

**IK weapon\_bone** represents the weapon animated pose parented to the head. Use this bone as a parent transform for weapons.

**IK hand\_r** and **IK hand\_l** are sed as IK targets for character arms. They are parented to the IK weapon\_bone, so when weapon is animated (e.g., by recoil or sway), hands will follow the gun correctly.

circle-check

**Tip**: Both weapon and hand bones are parented to the head to inherit rotations applied when looking around.

**IK weapon\_bone\_aim** is used for procedural aiming, and it defines the weapon idle pose. This game object has a [Dynamic Bone](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/character-animation-system/dynamic-bones)
 component attached to it:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FD42K0UqLekebBkNL5AjI%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5494f092-3806-4b08-8ce0-44f4f95e303c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c5223b91&sv=2)

Dynamic Bone.

The ik\_hand\_gun object is the weapon bone that we assigned in previous step. Simply put, it contains weapon movement.

The Dynamic Bone component will help preserve the weapon animated transform relative to the head bone. The Update Mode set to Preserve Overlay will ensure that this bone only uses the base idle pose.

#### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/fps-addon/quickstart/skeleton-and-ik#ik-weapon_bone_r)

IK weapon\_bone\_r

Additionally, the preset tool will create these game objects:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FkYlEGDtFZs2XiR72TR7X%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbae04c18-2e13-4bbd-82de-6342238f42d0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b67bf63b&sv=2)

Extra IK bones.

**IK weapon\_bone\_r** is a dynamic bone that contains weapon animated pose relative to the right hand.

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FstsW4Y0S9eDyXtKfhsN7%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D69b492e3-1d96-483c-9f4a-de96de0f466c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=196425dc&sv=2)

It is used to drive the IK weapon\_bone:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FrVZs3bt6JTtk2p7D8lHG%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3e5a0ff6-5387-4480-b27d-c2b2d8e8b985&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8ac34d62&sv=2)

Copy bone data.

circle-check

**Tip**: This setup lets us keep the animation relative to the right hand, then pas that to the IK weapon\_bone (parented to the head bone) and inherit rotations from the neck or spine bones.

#### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/fps-addon/quickstart/skeleton-and-ik#ik-hand_l_r)

IK hand\_l\_r

IK hand\_l\_r is another dynamic bone that represents the left hand pose relative to the right hand:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FJAUzt1ZwpC1RY49iTnQa%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7cd33450-ba3d-4b89-8152-5c0cf4f16603&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=463dc265&sv=2)

This bone is used to attach the left hand to the weapon:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252F2Paf3eGSUtAQVVeWFVDy%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De82783f6-759a-4b8a-bc5a-349a780cb6d5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=af6f4387&sv=2)

How it's used in the Attach Hand Modifier.

circle-info

**Tip**: The IK hand\_l\_r gets the left hand pose relative to the right hand, and then it gets passed to the [Attach Left Hand](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/fps-addon/modifiers/attach-hand)
 modifier.

# Recoil Animation | Character Animation System Docs

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/fps-addon/recoil-animation#recoil-animation-component)

Recoil Animation Component


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Recoil Animation** is a component that generates smooth and fluid firing animations at runtime:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FQO59MjqPrr3OFYxH0vmt%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df0b6e141-0bac-47ab-8066-c7fc0e53d537&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6c78d3dd&sv=2)

Recoil Animation component.

This component has 3 methods that need to be called in the shooting code:

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/fps-addon/recoil-animation#recoil-anim-data)

Recoil Anim Data


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Recoil parameters are defined in the RecoilAnimData — a Scriptable Object that can be created via **right-click ▸ Create ▸ KINEMATION ▸ Procedural Recoil ▸ Recoil Data**:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FpqfhORfkqopC7Dqr9cDX%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6d98b6bf-b90c-4cce-9364-51390114b26f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=46c6d6df&sv=2)

Recoil Anim Data properties.

Recoil Targets

Smoothing

Layers

Misc.

*   **Pitch** - max and min values for the pitch (up) rotation
    
*   **Roll** - max and min values for the roll rotation.
    
*   **Yaw** - max and min values for the yaw (right) rotation.
    

**Roll and Yaw** components are Vector4. That's because of the way random values are calculated:

Minimum value for **Roll and Yaw** is a random value in \[X;Y\] range, while the maximum value is in \[Z;W\] range.

**Aim Rot** and **Aim Loc** define multipliers for each rotation and translation. Applied when aiming.

**Smooth Rot/Loc** - defines interpolation speed for rotation and translation. Not applied if 0. **Extra Rot/Loc** - multipliers applied in auto/burst mode only.

Noise layer is a continuous 2D movement that simulates inaccuracy when firing.

*   **Noise X/Y** - max and min values for position offsets along X and Y axes (right and up movement).
    
*   **Noise Accel** - acceleration speed.
    
*   **Noise Damp** - damping speed. Noise Scalar - aiming multiplier.
    

Pushback layer is applied on the first shot of the auto or burst fire mode.

*   **Push Amount** - maximum value of the pushback.
    
*   **Push Accel** - acceleration speed.
    
*   **Push Damp** - damping speed.
    

*   **Hip Pivot Offset** - weapon pivot offset when hip firing.
    
*   **Aim Pivot Offset** - weapon pivot offset when aiming.
    
*   **Smooth Roll** - if enabled, the sign of a random value for roll will change every shot.
    
*   **Play Rate** - the speed of the recoil animation.
    
*   **Recoil Curves** - normalized animation curves.
    

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/fps-addon/recoil-animation#recoil-curves)

Recoil Curves


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

There are 4 Vector curves in the data asset, where each Vector curve is designed to animate the rotation or translation when auto/single firing.

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FTqqpOnphFBuztGs1XBzj%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D50d94766-aa3f-403e-8a86-d40d1c9a6a8a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=464b369d&sv=2)

Example semi curves.

circle-check

**Tip:** All curves must start and end with zero!

Here's the difference between auto and semi curves:

Semi

Auto

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252F0RQWyqFZqA2pYT5pTmlo%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7364edf3-202a-4c04-add0-b0a22f52ea4f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=67414256&sv=2)

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FJwCi73WZFGXoQlkt3yF5%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D01d73f2c-6ea7-4fc1-90cd-0783398bb42d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9e308f17&sv=2)

Curves are almost identical, the only difference is that the Auto curve value is very close to zero at some point - this point is the delay between shots.

> Example: let's say our fire rate is 600 RPM, then the delay between shots is 0.1s. This means, that all auto curves must be close to 0 at 0.1s time.

circle-info

**Tip:** This is required for the auto solver to work properly. When auto/burst mode is enabled, the curve length is set to the fire delay (see our example above). So, the length of the auto or burst curve gets cropped to the fire delay between shots.

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/fps-addon/recoil-animation#how-to-apply-recoil-animation)

How to apply recoil animation


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Add the Recoil Animation component to the character's prefab and apply the changes. Then, add a "Modify Bone" modifier to the Procedural Animation settings and bind recoil `OutRot` and `OutLoc` values:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FVcQ5dPCbxArDTGycBUfv%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4f54d201-8bbf-4776-8d42-eaea04719d30&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dbce8230&sv=2)

Modify Bone + Recoil Animation.

[PreviousWeapon Collisionchevron-left](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/fps-addon/modifiers/weapon-collision)
[NextFPSAF -> CAS Guidechevron-right](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/fps-addon/fpsaf-greater-than-cas-guide)

*   [Recoil Animation Component](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/fps-addon/recoil-animation#recoil-animation-component)
    
*   [Recoil Anim Data](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/fps-addon/recoil-animation#recoil-anim-data)
    
*   [Recoil Curves](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/fps-addon/recoil-animation#recoil-curves)
    
*   [How to apply recoil animation](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/fps-addon/recoil-animation#how-to-apply-recoil-animation)
    

Copy

    public void Play(); // Fired a gun, call it every shot.

Copy

    public void Stop(); // Call it when the fire key is released.

Copy

    // Call this when a gun is equipped.
    void Init(RecoilAnimData data, float fireRate, FireMode newFireMode);

# Weapon Collision | Character Animation System Docs

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/fps-addon/modifiers/weapon-collision#overview)

Overview


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Weapon Collision** is used to avoid weapon clipping with obstacles in the game world.

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FxZvpAfy9F9MDNmdkHFkr%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9facf6ca-55d9-4f6a-9cf7-ea62dec72ddb&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f80e76f0&sv=2)

*   **Pitch Input** is the vertical or look-up input value in range \[-90;90\].
    
*   **Primary Pose**/**Secondary Pose** are applied depending on the Pitch Input value. If it's greater than zero, Primary pose will be used — Secondary otherwise.
    
*   **Target Space** defines the space to apply the collision in. It is recommended to have this set to "Component".
    
*   **Interp Speed** is the smoothing speed. If set to zero, no smoothing will be applied.
    
*   **Layer Mask** defines What collision layers to include during a raycast.
    
*   **Start Offset** is the forward ray origin offset.
    
*   **Weapon Length** is the trace length. It's possible to bind a custom value from a player or weapon component to support different types of weapons.
    
*   **Trace Radius** is a sphere trace radius.
    

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/fps-addon/modifiers/weapon-collision#use-cases)

Use-cases


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This modifier is used to avoid collisions with obstacles. It's usually placed after the Look and after the IK modifiers:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FQbmRl05QWmANPS1xyeq9%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De475e193-1008-4185-bb28-98eed34b6a94&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e57f4682&sv=2)

[PreviousSway Modifierchevron-left](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/fps-addon/modifiers/sway-modifier)
[NextRecoil Animationchevron-right](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/fps-addon/recoil-animation)

Last updated 3 months ago

*   [Overview](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/fps-addon/modifiers/weapon-collision#overview)
    
*   [Use-cases](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/fps-addon/modifiers/weapon-collision#use-cases)

# IK Motions | Character Animation System Docs

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/fps-addon/modifiers/ik-motions#overview)

Overview


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**IK Motion** is a modifier that is used to play additive transition animations, like aiming for example.

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FULlkEkVKyA7ov0OXtRYn%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2c4cf5c5-dcbc-435c-9bfd-7a7ab3ebe26a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=71fdeb11&sv=2)

IK Motion modifier.

*   **Bone To Animate**: A Bone that will be animated by this motion.
    
*   **Rotation**/**Translation Curves**: Animation curves that will animate the bone.
    
*   **Rotation**/**Translation Scale**: Scale multipliers for each rotation/translation axis.
    
*   **Blend Time**: Blend in time in seconds.
    
*   **Play Rate**: Playback speed.
    
*   **Auto Blend Out**: Whether to automatically blend out the motion upon completion.
    

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/fps-addon/modifiers/ik-motions#use-cases)

Use-cases


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

IK Motion is used to play a dynamic additive animation on IK bones. For example, it can be used to add a "jiggle" effect when aiming.

Unlike other modifiers in CAS, IK Motion can be instantiated as a standalone Scriptable Object via right-click **Create/KINEMATION/CAS/Addons/FPS/IK Motion**.

To play an IK Motion in runtime, the `UpdateAnimationModifier` method should be used:

[PreviousFPS Offsetchevron-left](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/fps-addon/modifiers/fps-offset)
[NextAds Modifierchevron-right](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/fps-addon/modifiers/ads-modifier)

Last updated 3 months ago

*   [Overview](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/fps-addon/modifiers/ik-motions#overview)
    
*   [Use-cases](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/fps-addon/modifiers/ik-motions#use-cases)
    

Copy

    _characterAnimationComponent.UpdateAnimationModifier(newIkMotion);

---

# FPS Offset | Character Animation System Docs

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/fps-addon/modifiers/fps-offset#overview)

Overview


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This modifier lets you apply offsets to the weapon and hands IK targets:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FqYBwSaexO6dfEmbs6Hvn%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D89e915f0-f49b-47a4-af36-60650afcca3e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=72a9abe8&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/fps-addon/modifiers/fps-offset#bones)

Bones

*   Ik Weapon Bone is set to IK weapon\_bone, and it represents the weapon animated pose.
    
*   Ik Weapon Bone Aim represents the weapon default idle pose, which is used for aiming.
    
*   Ik Hand Right/Left is an IK bone target for the right/left hand.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/fps-addon/modifiers/fps-offset#offsets)

Offsets

*   **Weapon Bone Offset** is a rotation and translation offset for the Ik Weapon Bone in component space.
    
*   **Right**/**Left Hand Offset** is a rotation and translation offset for the Ik Right/Left Hand relative to the weapon.
    

[hashtag](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/fps-addon/modifiers/fps-offset#use-cases)

Use-cases


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This modifier is generally used to adjust the weapon pose in first-person view. It's recommended to bind offset values from a scriptable objects, character controller or a weapon:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FACo2H4NTT7ddzJHcaI9F%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df27effc4-ef30-48f2-8739-7eaaa8cba9ee&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e8b10869&sv=2)

Exanple from the demo content.

In the FPS Addon Demo, weapon animation data is stored in a scriptable object. This **FPS Offset** modifier links that data asset with the animation system.

**FPS Offset** is usually placed after the [FPS Copy Bones](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/fps-addon/modifiers/fps-copy-bones)
, additional Copy Bone, and the Attach Hand modifiers:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FTdicva41NDW2IS5ZBLbF%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1d241f97-c4dc-477a-adaf-cb2a8044d568&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fb636fe9&sv=2)

It's also possible to add multiple FPS Offsets to the same Procedural Animation Settings asset:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FFRdsOV2wNRSYtNvQCeX4%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4c74018d-9395-48eb-b024-c13302f496ec&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5d8d800a&sv=2)

Multiple FPS Offsets from the demo.

In this example, there're 3 offset modifiers used for different gameplay situations. To make these modifiers active only in certain situations, use the Weight Overrides feature:

![](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1519747473-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrZsugF4ifwEvaFE7BvLB%252Fuploads%252FuSScq8HO7gBO7xs3Qc85%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D93d79510-4094-45eb-911d-f761668fc13e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e719eed0&sv=2)

Weight Overrides.

This override will activate the modifier only when the player is in first-person view.

[PreviousAttach Handchevron-left](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/fps-addon/modifiers/attach-hand)
[NextIK Motionschevron-right](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/fps-addon/modifiers/ik-motions)

Last updated 3 months ago

*   [Overview](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/fps-addon/modifiers/fps-offset#overview)
    
*   [Use-cases](https://kinemation.gitbook.io/character-animation-system-docs/fps-addon/modifiers/fps-offset#use-cases)
